-- ============================================================
-- 2. Setup services and variables
-- ============================================================
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local playerName = player.Name

-- Store owned badges
local ownedBadges = {}

-- ============================================================
-- 3. Fetch owned badges from ReplicatedStorage (PARSE ARRAY FORMAT)
-- ============================================================
local function fetchOwnedBadges()
    ownedBadges = {}
    
    -- Build the path to the player's UnlockedBadges folder
    local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
    if not playerData then
        warn("PlayerData not found in ReplicatedStorage")
        return false
    end
    
    local playerFolder = playerData:FindFirstChild(playerName)
    if not playerFolder then
        warn("Player folder not found for: " .. playerName)
        return false
    end
    
    local unlockedBadges = playerFolder:FindFirstChild("UnlockedBadges")
    if not unlockedBadges then
        warn("UnlockedBadges not found for: " .. playerName)
        return false
    end
    
    -- Get the value (format: [2124743766,3713925567966983,2124760923,...])
    if unlockedBadges:IsA("StringValue") then
        local badgeIdsString = unlockedBadges.Value
        
        if badgeIdsString and badgeIdsString ~= "" then
            -- Parse the array format [id1, id2, id3]
            -- Remove the brackets [ and ]
            local trimmed = badgeIdsString:sub(2, -2) -- Remove first and last character
            
            -- Split by commas
            local badgeIds = {}
            for id in string.gmatch(trimmed, "[^,]+") do
                -- Remove any whitespace and convert to string for consistent comparison
                local cleanId = id:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
                table.insert(badgeIds, cleanId)
            end
            
            -- Mark all owned badges as true
            for _, id in ipairs(badgeIds) do
                ownedBadges[id] = true
            end
            
        else
        end
        return true
    else
        return false
    end
end

-- ============================================================
-- 4. Build the formatted display text
-- ============================================================
local function getFormattedBadgeList()
    local categories = {
        Miscellaneous = {},
        Limited = {},
        Double = {},
        Normal = {},
    }

    for _, badge in ipairs(allBadges) do
        local cat = categories[badge.category] or categories.Normal
        table.insert(cat, badge)
    end

    local totalCount = #allBadges
    local ownedCount = 0
    for _, badge in ipairs(allBadges) do
        if ownedBadges[badge.id] then
            ownedCount = ownedCount + 1
        end
    end

    local lines = {}
    local function push(s) table.insert(lines, s) end

    local function section(title, icon, list)
        push("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━")
        push("              " .. icon .. " " .. title .. " " .. icon)
        push("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━")
        for _, badge in ipairs(list) do
            local status = ownedBadges[badge.id] and "✅" or "❌"
            push(status .. " " .. badge.name)
        end
        push("")
    end

    section("MISCELLANEOUS BADGES", "🏆", categories.Miscellaneous)
    section("LIMITED BADGES", "🎯", categories.Limited)
    section("DOUBLE BADGES", "⚡", categories.Double)
    section("NORMAL BADGES", "📜", categories.Normal)

    push("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━")
    push("              📊 STATISTICS 📊")
    push("━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━")
    push("✅ Owned: " .. ownedCount .. "/" .. totalCount)
    push("❌ Missing: " .. (totalCount - ownedCount) .. "/" .. totalCount)
    push(string.format("📈 Progress: %.1f%%", (ownedCount / totalCount) * 100))

    return table.concat(lines, "\n")
end

            fetchOwnedBadges()

        end)
    end

    task.wait(1)
    fetchOwnedBadges()
    badgeParagraph:Set(getFormattedBadgeList())
    
    while true do
        task.wait(0.01) -- Update every 10 seconds
        fetchOwnedBadges()
        badgeParagraph:Set(getFormattedBadgeList())
    end
end)

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "MEGAROCK",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
})

-- Variables for tracking
local timeStarted = nil
local timeStopped = nil
local isCounting = false
local isRockActive = false
local totalTimeNeeded = 10 * 60 * 60 -- 10 hours in seconds (36000 Seconds)
local rockStartTime = nil
local isTimerFinished = false
local updateConnection = nil
local currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for Rock..."
local currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
local currentTimeStopped = "N/A"
local currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
local savedStoppedTime = nil
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local autoMegarockEnabled = false
local autoMegarockLoop = nil
local isProcessing = false -- Prevents double firing

-- Badge tracking variables
local ownsReallyBadge = false
local ownsWHYBadge = false
local reallyBadgeAward = "No Glove"
local whyBadgeAward = "MEGAROCK Glove"

-- Badge IDs
local REALLY_BADGE_ID = 2124760923 -- "really?" badge
local WHY_BADGE_ID = 2124807768 -- "WHY" badge (MEGAROCK Glove)

-- Function to format time (Hours:Minutes:Seconds:Milliseconds)
local function formatTime(seconds, milliseconds)
    local hours = math.floor(seconds / 3600)
    local minutes = math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60)
    local secs = math.floor(seconds % 60)
    local ms = math.floor(milliseconds or 0)
    return string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d:%03d", hours, minutes, secs, ms)
end

-- Function to check if a badge is owned
local function checkBadge(badgeId)
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == badgeId then
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to update badge statuses
local function updateBadgeStatuses()
    -- Check "really?" badge (ID: 2124760923)
    ownsReallyBadge = checkBadge(REALLY_BADGE_ID)
    
    -- Check "WHY" badge (ID: 2124807768)
    ownsWHYBadge = checkBadge(WHY_BADGE_ID)
end

-- Function to get formatted badge status text
local function getFormattedBadgeStatus()
    local statusText = string.format([[
Owns really? Badge: %s
Owns WHY Badge: %s
really? Badge Awards Glove: %s
WHY Badge Awards Glove: %s
]],
    ownsReallyBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No",
    ownsWHYBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No",
    reallyBadgeAward,
    whyBadgeAward
)
    return statusText
end

-- Optimized function to check for rock
local function hasRock()
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    local character = player and player.Character
    if character then
        return character:FindFirstChild("rock") ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if diamond glove is EQUIPPED
local function isDiamondEquipped()
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    local character = player and player.Character
    if character then
        local diamondTool = character:FindFirstChild("Diamond")
        if diamondTool then
            return true
        end
    end
    return false
end

-- Timer update function (FAST - updates every 0.1 seconds)
local function updateTimerDisplay(paragraph)
    local currentTime = tick()
    local hasRockNow = hasRock()
    local diamondEquipped = isDiamondEquipped()
    
    -- Time Waiting logic (just waits, doesn't start timer)
    if not hasRockNow then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for Rock..."
    else
        currentTimeWaiting = "Rock Found!"
    end
    
    -- Time Started / Time Stopped / Time Finished logic
    if hasRockNow then
        if not isRockActive then
            -- Rock just appeared - START the timer
            isRockActive = true
            rockStartTime = currentTime
            isCounting = true
            isTimerFinished = false
            timeStarted = rockStartTime
            savedStoppedTime = nil
            currentTimeStopped = "N/A"
            -- Show the start time as 0
            currentTimeStarted = formatTime(0, 0)
        end
        
        if isCounting and not isTimerFinished then
            local elapsed = currentTime - rockStartTime
            local milliseconds = (elapsed - math.floor(elapsed)) * 1000
            currentTimeStarted = formatTime(elapsed, milliseconds)
            
            -- Check if reached 10 hours
            if elapsed >= totalTimeNeeded then
                isTimerFinished = true
                isCounting = false
                currentTimeFinished = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
            end
        elseif isTimerFinished then
            currentTimeFinished = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
            currentTimeStarted = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
        end
    else
        -- Rock disappeared
        if isRockActive then
            -- Save the time when rock disappeared
            isRockActive = false
            isCounting = false
            savedStoppedTime = currentTimeStarted
            currentTimeStopped = savedStoppedTime
        end
        -- Keep showing the saved stopped time, don't reset to N/A
        if savedStoppedTime then
            currentTimeStopped = savedStoppedTime
        end
        -- Reset timer variables so next rock starts fresh
        if not isRockActive and not hasRockNow then
            -- Only reset if we're not going to immediately start again
            isCounting = false
        end
    end
    
    -- Format the paragraph content (ONLY timer info, no badge stuff)
    local paragraphContent = string.format([[
Auto Rock Time Waiting: %s
Auto Rock Time Started: %s
Auto Rock Time Stopped: %s
Auto Rock Time Finished: %s
Total Time Need: %s
Diamond Glove Equipped: %s
Anti AFK: %s
]], 
    currentTimeWaiting,
    currentTimeStarted,
    currentTimeStopped,
    currentTimeFinished,
    formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0),
    diamondEquipped and "Yes" or "No",
    isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
)
    
    -- Update paragraph
    pcall(function()
        paragraph:Set(paragraphContent)
    end)
end

-- Create the paragraphs
local RestStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("MEGAROCK Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- FAST update loop for timer (every 0.1 seconds)
local isUpdating = true
task.spawn(function()
    while isUpdating do
        local startTime = tick()
        updateTimerDisplay(RestStatusParagraph)
        local elapsed = tick() - startTime
        local waitTime = math.max(0.01, 0.01 - elapsed)
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end)

-- SLOW update loop for badges (every 5 seconds - saves performance)
task.spawn(function()
    -- Initial badge check
    updateBadgeStatuses()
    BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(getFormattedBadgeStatus())
    
    -- Update every 5 seconds (badges don't change often)
    while isUpdating do
        task.wait(2)
        updateBadgeStatuses()
        BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(getFormattedBadgeStatus())
    end
end)

-- Function to fire rock remote (with cooldown to prevent double firing)
local function fireRockRemote()
    if isProcessing then
        return false -- Already processing
    end
    
    isProcessing = true
    
    pcall(function()
        local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
        local rockmode = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("Rockmode")
        if rockmode then
            rockmode:FireServer()
            task.wait(0.5)
        end
    end)
    
    task.wait(1) -- Cooldown to prevent double firing
    isProcessing = false
    return true
end

-- Auto Megarock Loop
local function startAutoMegarockLoop()
    autoMegarockLoop = task.spawn(function()
        while autoMegarockEnabled do
            pcall(function()
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local hasRockNow = hasRock()
                
                if not hasRockNow then
                    -- No rock, teleport and fire remote (with cooldown)
                    if player and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-17926, 60, 3531)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        fireRockRemote()
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end
            end)
            task.wait(3) -- Check every 3 seconds (reduces double firing)
        end
    end)
end

AutoMegarock = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Get MEGAROCK Glove",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        -- Prevent running if already in this state
        if autoMegarockEnabled == Value then
            return
        end
        
        autoMegarockEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            
            -- Check if player already has rock
            if hasRock() then
                -- Has rock, disable toggle (don't auto-disable, just notify)
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "MEGAROCK",
                    Content = "You already have Rock! Disable the toggle when you want to remove it.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                -- Don't auto-disable, let user manually disable
            else
                -- No rock, start the process
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "MEGAROCK",
                    Content = "Auto Get MEGAROCK Enabled! Teleporting to position...",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                
                -- Teleport and fire remote once immediately (with cooldown)
                if player and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-17926, 60, 3531)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                    fireRockRemote()
                end
                
                -- Stop existing loop if any
                if autoMegarockLoop then
                    task.cancel(autoMegarockLoop)
                    autoMegarockLoop = nil
                end
                
                -- Start the loop to keep trying (only if still enabled)
                if autoMegarockEnabled then
                    startAutoMegarockLoop()
                end
            end
        else
            -- Disable toggle - ONLY fire remote if user has rock
            if hasRock() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "MEGAROCK",
                    Content = "Disabling MEGAROCK...",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 2
                })
                
                -- Run remote to disable MEGAROCK
                fireRockRemote()
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "MEGAROCK",
                    Content = "MEGAROCK Disabled.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 2
                })
            end
            
            -- Stop the loop
            if autoMegarockLoop then
                task.cancel(autoMegarockLoop)
                autoMegarockLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

-- Cleanup when script stops
game.Players.LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function()
    isUpdating = false
    if autoMegarockLoop then
        task.cancel(autoMegarockLoop)
    end
end)

end

        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Plague" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end

        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Plague Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({

    Callback = function()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Killstreak" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Right Arm"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Right Arm"]
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Right Arm" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.KSHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Killstreak",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Grave ESP",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        GraveESP = Value

        if not Value then
            -- Remove ESP from Grave
            local grave = workspace:FindFirstChild("Gravestone")
            if grave and grave:IsA("Model") then
                local gui = grave:FindFirstChild("GraveESP")
                if gui then gui:Destroy() end
            end
            return
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            while GraveESP do
                local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local char = lp.Character
                local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

                if hrp then
                    -- Grave ESP
                    local graveTarget = workspace:FindFirstChild("Gravestone")
                    if graveTarget and graveTarget:IsA("Model") then
                        local gui = graveTarget:FindFirstChild("GraveESP")

                        -- Create ESP for Grave
                        if not gui then
                            gui = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
                            gui.Name = "GraveESP"
                            gui.Adornee = graveTarget
                            gui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 150, 0, 40)
                            gui.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                            gui.AlwaysOnTop = true
                            gui.Parent = graveTarget

                            local label = Instance.new("TextLabel", gui)
                            label.Name = "Label"
                            label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                            label.TextSize = 16
                            label.Font = Enum.Font.FredokaOne
                            label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0) -- Red
                            label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.2
                            label.Text = "Grave"
                        end

                        -- Update distance for Grave
                        local label = gui:FindFirstChild("Label")
                        if label then
                            local dist = math.floor((graveTarget:GetPivot().Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude)
                            label.Text = "Grave | " .. dist .. "m"
                        end
                    end
                end

                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end
})

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "[REDACTED]",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Get [REDACTED] Glove",
    Callback = function()
        task.spawn(function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            
            -- Check slaps requirement
            if player.leaderstats.Slaps.Value < 0 then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "0+ Slaps Required", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
                return
            end
            
            -- Keep running until badge is obtained
            local badgeId = 2124847850
            local hasBadge = false
            
            repeat
                -- Wait for character to load
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then
                    character = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    task.wait(1)
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then
                    hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                end
                
                -- Bring every object from Doors folder
                for _, obj in pairs(workspace.PocketDimension.Doors:GetChildren()) do
                    pcall(function()
                        if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                            local originalCFrame = obj.CFrame
                            local originalAnchored = obj.Anchored
                            
                            obj.Anchored = false
                            obj.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                            task.wait(0.05)
                            obj.CFrame = originalCFrame
                            obj.Anchored = originalAnchored
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.05)
                end
                
                -- Check if badge was obtained
                pcall(function()
                    hasBadge = game:GetService("BadgeService"):UserHasBadgeAsync(player.UserId, badgeId)
                end)
                
                task.wait(0.02) -- Small delay before next loop
                
            until hasBadge == true
            
            -- Notify success
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Success", Content = "Glove obtained!", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
        end)
    end    
})

end

Tab:AddButton({

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "bus" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "bus Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Bring Bus",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value) 
        Giftfarm = Value
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while Giftfarm do
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if not player then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                -- Find BusModel
                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "BusModel" then
                        pcall(function()
                            -- Method 1: Teleport the bus to the player (brings bus to you)
                            local busPrimaryPart = v:FindFirstChild("PrimaryPart") or v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or v:FindFirstChild("RootPart")
                            
                            if busPrimaryPart then
                                -- Move bus to player's position
                                busPrimaryPart.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                            else
                                -- If no primary part, move the whole model
                                local modelParts = {}
                                for _, part in pairs(v:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                        table.insert(modelParts, part)
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                -- Move each part to player
                                for _, part in pairs(modelParts) do
                                    part.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                            
                            -- Alternative: Move player to bus (if you want player to go to bus)
                            -- hrp.CFrame = v:GetPivot() + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                        end)
                    end
                end
                
                task.wait(0.05) -- Faster than original for better collection
            end
        end)
    end
})

end

Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Warp",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Get Warp Glove",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Swapper" and not game:GetService("BadgeService"):UserHasBadgeAsync(game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId, 0) then
if _G.ClosestMagnitude == nil then
_G.ClosestMagnitude = 999999
end
repeat
for _, v in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
if v ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v.Character and v.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
local Magnitude = (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
if Magnitude <= _G.ClosestMagnitude then
if v.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") == nil or v.Character.Humanoid.Health == 0 then
_G.ClosestMagnitude = 999999
RandomPlayer = nil
else
_G.ClosestMagnitude = Magnitude
RandomPlayer = v
end
end
end
end
if RandomPlayer and _G.ClosestMagnitude ~= 999999 then
if RandomPlayer ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and RandomPlayer.Character then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and RandomPlayer.Character.Ragdolled.Value == false then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head").CFrame
wait(0.17)
game.ReplicatedStorage.HitSwapper:FireServer(RandomPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Head"))
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["SafeBox"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0,5,0)
end
end
end
task.wait(0.15)
until RandomPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Y < -10
wait(0.2)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame * CFrame.new(0,10,0)
wait(0.15)
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SLOC:FireServer()
wait(0.2)
if _G.ClosestMagnitude and RandomPlayer then
_G.ClosestMagnitude = nil
RandomPlayer = nil
end
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Swapper",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
  	end    
})

end

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Bubble",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

-- Global flag to control loop
_G.KillstreakSlapRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players (Killstreak)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.KillstreakSlapRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player (not self)
        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                end
            else
                warn("Not enough players to teleport.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire GeneralHit on all players
        local function fireKSHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage.KSHit:FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoSlapKillstreakLoop()
            if LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Killstreak" then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Killstreak glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.KillstreakSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.KillstreakSlapRunning do
                wait(0.5)
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireKSHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoSlapKillstreakLoop)()
        else
            _G.KillstreakSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Killstreak Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Killstreak" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Right Arm"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Right Arm"]
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Right Arm" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.KSHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Killstreak",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

-- Global flag to control loop
_G.DisarmSlapRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players (Reaper)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.DisarmSlapRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player (not self)
        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            else
                warn("Not enough players to teleport.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire ReaperHit on all players
        local function fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("ReaperHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoDisarmSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Reaper") then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Disarm glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.DisarmSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoDisarmSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

            if player ~= localPlayer then

-- Global flag to control loop
_G.SnowOverkillRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap OVERKILL Players (Snow)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.SnowOverkillRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player with OVERKILL (not self)
        local function teleportToOverkillPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            local overkillPlayers = {}
            
            -- Find all players with OVERKILL
            for _, player in pairs(playerList) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" then
                        table.insert(overkillPlayers, player)
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if #overkillPlayers > 0 then
                local randomPlayer = overkillPlayers[math.random(1, #overkillPlayers)]
                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            else
                warn("No players with OVERKILL found.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire Snow hits on OVERKILL players only
        local function fireSnowHitForOverkillPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" and player.Character then
                        local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                        if rightArm then
                            ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("SnowHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoSnowOverkillLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Snow") then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Snow glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.SnowOverkillRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.SnowOverkillRunning do
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                teleportToOverkillPlayer()
                fireSnowHitForOverkillPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoSnowOverkillLoop)()
        else
            _G.SnowOverkillRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Snow Slap Aura (OVERKILL Players Only)",
    Callback = function()   
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Snow" then
            -- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            -- Start the infinite loop to fire for OVERKILL players only
            while true do
                -- Loop through each player in the game
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    -- Check if player has OVERKILL glove
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                        local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                        local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                        
                        -- Only target players with OVERKILL glove
                        if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
                            local args = {
                                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                            }

                            -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
                            ReplicatedStorage.SnowHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end

                -- Wait 0.5 seconds before running the loop again
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "Equip Snow", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
        end
    end
})

				-- Check for Reverse glove
				if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Reverse" then
					OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "Equip Reverse/Use Ability", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
					Potatofarm = false
					break
				end
				
				local character = player.Character
				if not character or not character.Parent then 
					task.wait(0.01) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if not hrp then 
					task.wait(0.01) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local bubblesFound = 0
				
				-- Find all BubbleObjects
				for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
					if v.Name == "BubbleObject" then
						bubblesFound = bubblesFound + 1
						pcall(function()
							-- Teleport bubble directly to player's HRP
							if v:IsA("BasePart") then
								-- Bubble is a single part
								v.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
							elseif v:IsA("Model") then
								-- Bubble is a model
								local bubblePart = v:FindFirstChild("Handle") or v:FindFirstChild("BubblePart") or v:FindFirstChild("PrimaryPart")
								
								if bubblePart then
									bubblePart.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
								else
									-- Move all parts to player
									for _, part in pairs(v:GetDescendants()) do
										if part:IsA("BasePart") then
											part.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
										end
									end
								end
							end
						end)
					end
				end
				
				-- Adjust wait time based on whether bubbles were found
				if bubblesFound == 0 then
					task.wait(0.3) -- No bubbles, wait a bit
				else
					task.wait(0.05) -- Bubbles found, fast loop
				end
			end
		end)
	end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "CULT",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto potato Slap Aura",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "potato" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Arm"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.potatohit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip potato",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "bob",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- ===== VARIABLES =====
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local cloneCount = 0
local isSpawning = false
local spawnStarted = false
local spawnStopped = false
local spawnFinished = false
local legitCloneCount = 0
local legitSpawning = false
local legitSpawnStarted = false
local legitSpawnStopped = false
local legitSpawnFinished = false
local totalClonesNeeded = 7500
local ownBobBadge = false
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local isReplicaEquipped = false

-- Bob Badge ID
local BOB_BADGE_ID = 2125950512

-- Function to check if Replica glove is equipped
local function checkReplicaGlove()
    if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
        isReplicaEquipped = (player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Replica")
        return isReplicaEquipped
    end
    isReplicaEquipped = false
    return false
end

-- Function to check if Bob badge is owned
local function checkBobBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == BOB_BADGE_ID then
                    ownBobBadge = true
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    ownBobBadge = false
    return false
end

-- Function to format status text for Exploit Mode
local function getExploitStatusText()
    local waitingStatus = "Waiting to start..."
    local startedStatus = "Not Started"
    local stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
    local finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    
    if spawnFinished then
        waitingStatus = "Finished!"
        startedStatus = "7500/7500"
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "7500/7500"
    elseif spawnStopped then
        waitingStatus = "Stopped"
        startedStatus = cloneCount .. "/" .. totalClonesNeeded
        stoppedStatus = cloneCount .. "/" .. totalClonesNeeded
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    elseif spawnStarted then
        waitingStatus = "Running..."
        startedStatus = cloneCount .. "/" .. totalClonesNeeded
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    elseif not isSpawning then
        waitingStatus = "Ready to start"
        startedStatus = "Not Started"
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    end
    
    local replicaStatus = isReplicaEquipped and "Yes" or "No"
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    local percentage = 0.013
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Clone Auto Spawn Waiting: %s
Clone Auto Spawn Started: %s
Clone Auto Spawn Stopped: %s
Clone Auto Spawn Finished: %s
Total Clones Need To Be Spawned: %d
Total Percentage For Bob To Spawn: %.3f%%
Replica Glove Equipped: %s
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    waitingStatus,
    startedStatus,
    stoppedStatus,
    finishedStatus,
    totalClonesNeeded,
    percentage,
    replicaStatus,
    antiAfkStatus
)
    return statusText
end

-- Function to format status text for Legit Mode
local function getLegitStatusText()
    local waitingStatus = "Waiting to start..."
    local startedStatus = "Not Started"
    local stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
    local finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    
    if legitSpawnFinished then
        waitingStatus = "Finished!"
        startedStatus = "7500/7500"
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "7500/7500"
    elseif legitSpawnStopped then
        waitingStatus = "Stopped"
        startedStatus = legitCloneCount .. "/" .. totalClonesNeeded
        stoppedStatus = legitCloneCount .. "/" .. totalClonesNeeded
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    elseif legitSpawnStarted then
        waitingStatus = "Running..."
        startedStatus = legitCloneCount .. "/" .. totalClonesNeeded
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    elseif not legitSpawning then
        waitingStatus = "Ready to start"
        startedStatus = "Not Started"
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    end
    
    local replicaStatus = isReplicaEquipped and "Yes" or "No"
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    local percentage = 0.013
    local badgeStatus = ownBobBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No"
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Clone Auto Spawn Waiting: %s
Clone Auto Spawn Started: %s
Clone Auto Spawn Stopped: %s
Clone Auto Spawn Finished: %s
Total Clones Need To Be Spawned: %d
Total Percentage For Bob To Spawn: %.3f%%
Replica Glove Equipped: %s
Anti AFK: %s
Owns bob Badge: %s
bob Badge Awards Glove: bob Glove
]],
    waitingStatus,
    startedStatus,
    stoppedStatus,
    finishedStatus,
    totalClonesNeeded,
    percentage,
    replicaStatus,
    antiAfkStatus,
    badgeStatus
)
    return statusText
end

-- Create paragraphs
local ExploitStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Exploit Mode Status:", "Loading...")
local LegitStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Legit Mode Status:", "Loading...")

-- Function to spawn clone (Exploit Mode - kills character)
local function spawnCloneExploit()
    if not isSpawning then return end
    
    pcall(function()
        if checkReplicaGlove() then
            local char = player.Character
            if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                
                local teleport1 = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("Teleport1")
                if teleport1 then
                    char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = teleport1.CFrame
                    task.wait(0.2)
                end
                
                local duplicate = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("Duplicate")
                if duplicate then
                    duplicate:FireServer(true)
                    task.wait(0.2)
                end
                
                if char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                    char.Humanoid.Health = 0
                end
                
                if not spawnFinished then
                    cloneCount = cloneCount + 1
                end
                
                if cloneCount >= totalClonesNeeded then
                    spawnFinished = true
                    isSpawning = false
                    spawnStarted = false
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end

-- Function to spawn clone (Legit Mode - spawns clone then waits)
local legitSpawningInProgress = false

local function spawnCloneLegit()
    if not legitSpawning then return end
    if legitSpawningInProgress then return end
    legitSpawningInProgress = true
    
    pcall(function()
        if checkReplicaGlove() then
            local char = player.Character
            if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                
                local teleport1 = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("Teleport1")
                if teleport1 then
                    local hrp = char.HumanoidRootPart
                    local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                    local distance = (hrp.Position - teleport1.Position).Magnitude
                    
                    if distance > 5 then
                        -- Walk to teleport
                        humanoid:MoveTo(teleport1.Position)
                        
                        -- Wait until close enough
                        local attempts = 0
                        while (hrp.Position - teleport1.Position).Magnitude > 5 and attempts < 50 do
                            task.wait(0.1)
                            attempts = attempts + 1
                            char = player.Character
                            if not char then break end
                            hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                            if not hrp or not humanoid then break end
                            humanoid:MoveTo(teleport1.Position)
                        end
                        task.wait(0.2)
                    end
                    
                    -- Teleport to exact position
                    hrp.CFrame = teleport1.CFrame
                    task.wait(0.3)
                end
                
                -- Fire duplicate remote to spawn clone
                local duplicate = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("Duplicate")
                if duplicate then
                    duplicate:FireServer(true)
                    task.wait(1)
                end
                
                -- Update clone count
                if not legitSpawnFinished then
                    legitCloneCount = legitCloneCount + 1
                end
                
                -- Check if finished
                if legitCloneCount >= totalClonesNeeded then
                    legitSpawnFinished = true
                    legitSpawning = false
                    legitSpawnStarted = false
                end
                
                -- CRITICAL FIX: Wait for clone to be created before next spawn
                task.wait(2)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    legitSpawningInProgress = false
end

-- Function to wait for respawn (Exploit Mode)
local function waitForRespawn()
    if player.Character then
        local humanoid = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        if humanoid and humanoid.Health <= 0 then
            player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
            task.wait(1)
            return true
        end
    end
    return false
end

-- Reset functions
local function resetExploitMode()
    cloneCount = 0
    isSpawning = false
    spawnStarted = false
    spawnStopped = false
    spawnFinished = false
end

local function resetLegitMode()
    legitCloneCount = 0
    legitSpawning = false
    legitSpawnStarted = false
    legitSpawnStopped = false
    legitSpawnFinished = false
    legitSpawningInProgress = false
end

-- ===== EXPLOIT MODE TOGGLE =====
local exploitModeEnabled = false
local exploitLoop = nil

local function startExploitMode()
    exploitLoop = task.spawn(function()
        while exploitModeEnabled and not spawnFinished do
            pcall(function()
                if not player.Character then
                    player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    task.wait(1)
                end
                
                local char = player.Character
                local humanoid = char and char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                
                if humanoid and humanoid.Health <= 0 then
                    waitForRespawn()
                    return
                end
                
                if checkReplicaGlove() then
                    spawnCloneExploit()
                end
            end)
            task.wait(0.5)
        end
    end)
end

local exploitToggle = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Get Bob Glove (Exploit Mode)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        exploitModeEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            if checkReplicaGlove() then
                resetExploitMode()
                isSpawning = true
                spawnStarted = true
                spawnStopped = false
                spawnFinished = false
                
                if exploitLoop then
                    task.cancel(exploitLoop)
                end
                startExploitMode()
                
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Exploit Mode",
                    Content = "Started! Will spawn " .. totalClonesNeeded .. " clones",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Replica Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                exploitToggle:Set(false)
                exploitModeEnabled = false
            end
        else
            if exploitLoop then
                task.cancel(exploitLoop)
                exploitLoop = nil
            end
            isSpawning = false
            spawnStopped = true
            spawnStarted = false
            
        end
    end
})

-- ===== LEGIT MODE TOGGLE =====
local legitModeEnabled = false
local legitLoop = nil
local legitKillEnabled = true  -- Optional: set to true if you want to kill character

local function startLegitMode()
    legitLoop = task.spawn(function()
        while legitModeEnabled and not legitSpawnFinished do
            pcall(function()
                if not player.Character then
                    player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    task.wait(2)
                end
                
                local char = player.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    if checkReplicaGlove() then
                        if not legitSpawningInProgress then
                            spawnCloneLegit()
                            
                            -- OPTIONAL: Kill character to reset position (makes it like exploit mode but without remote kill)
                            -- Set legitKillEnabled = true at the top if you want this behavior
                            if legitKillEnabled then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid.Health = 0
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
            task.wait(0.5)
        end
    end)
end

local legitToggle = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Get Bob Glove (Legit Mode) [Buggy]",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        legitModeEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            if checkReplicaGlove() then
                resetLegitMode()
                legitSpawning = true
                legitSpawnStarted = true
                legitSpawnStopped = false
                legitSpawnFinished = false
                
                if legitLoop then
                    task.cancel(legitLoop)
                end
                startLegitMode()

            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Replica Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                legitToggle:Set(false)
                legitModeEnabled = false
            end
        else
            if legitLoop then
                task.cancel(legitLoop)
                legitLoop = nil
            end
            legitSpawning = false
            legitSpawnStopped = true
            legitSpawnStarted = false
            legitSpawningInProgress = false
            
        end
    end
})

AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti AFK",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')

                VirtualUser:CaptureController()

            end)
        end
    end    
})

-- ===== CONSTANT UPDATE LOOP =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local startTime = tick()
        
        checkReplicaGlove()
        checkBobBadge()
        
        ExploitStatusParagraph:Set(getExploitStatusText())
        LegitStatusParagraph:Set(getLegitStatusText())
        
        local elapsed = tick() - startTime
        local waitTime = math.max(0.01, 0.05 - elapsed)
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end)

--[[ This script isn't mine but idk how to create one so i use this instead ]]-- 
local AllIDs = {}
local foundAnything = ""
local actualHour = os.date("!*t").hour
local Deleted = false
local S_T = game:GetService("TeleportService")
local S_H = game:GetService("HttpService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local File = pcall(function()
    AllIDs = S_H:JSONDecode(readfile("server-hop-temp.json"))
end)
if not File then
    table.insert(AllIDs, actualHour)
    pcall(function()
        writefile("server-hop-temp.json", S_H:JSONEncode(AllIDs))
    end)
end

local function TPReturner(placeId)
    local Site
    if foundAnything == "" then
        Site = S_H:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. placeId .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100'))
    else
        Site = S_H:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. placeId .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor=' .. foundAnything))
    end

    local ID = ""
    if Site.nextPageCursor and Site.nextPageCursor ~= "null" and Site.nextPageCursor ~= nil then
        foundAnything = Site.nextPageCursor
    end

    local num = 0
    local foundServer = false 

    for i, v in pairs(Site.data) do
        local Possible = true
        ID = tostring(v.id)
        if tonumber(v.maxPlayers) > tonumber(v.playing) then
            for _, Existing in pairs(AllIDs) do
                if num ~= 0 then
                    if ID == tostring(Existing) then
                        Possible = false
                    end
                else
                    if tonumber(actualHour) ~= tonumber(Existing) then
                        local delFile = pcall(function()
                            delfile("server-hop-temp.json")
                            AllIDs = {}
                            table.insert(AllIDs, actualHour)
                        end)
                    end
                end
                num = num + 1
            end
            if Possible == true then
                table.insert(AllIDs, ID)
                foundServer = true
                wait()
                pcall(function()
                    writefile("server-hop-temp.json", S_H:JSONEncode(AllIDs))
                    wait()
                    S_T:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, ID, Players.LocalPlayer)
                end)
                wait(4)
            end
        end
    end

    -- if not found server
    if not foundServer then
        game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(game.PlaceId)
    end
end

local module = {}
function module:Teleport(placeId)
    while wait() do
        pcall(function()
            TPReturner(placeId)
            if foundAnything ~= "" then
                TPReturner(placeId)
            end
        end)
    end
end


module:Teleport(game.PlaceId)
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "65000+ Slaps Required",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
task.wait(0.05)
AutoGetBobGlove:Set(false)
end
end
})

    Name = "Instant Spawn 75k Clones (God Hand Uses Your Friend/Alt)",
    Callback = function()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Replica" then
wait(0.1)
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Lobby.Teleport1.CFrame
task.wait(1)
for i = 1, 75000 do
        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Duplicate:FireServer(unpack({[1] = true}))
end
wait(9)

local module = {}
function module:Teleport(placeId)
    while wait() do
        pcall(function()
            TPReturner(placeId)
            if foundAnything ~= "" then
                TPReturner(placeId)
            end
        end)
    end
end

module:Teleport(game.PlaceId)
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Replica Glove",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end

-- Global flag to control loop
_G.GoldenSlapRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.GoldenSlapRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player (not self)
        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            else
                warn("Not enough players to teleport.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire GoldenHit on all players
        local function fireGoldenHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("GoldenHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoGoldenSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Golden") then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Golden glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.GoldenSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.GoldenSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireGoldenHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoGoldenSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.GoldenSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Golden" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Leg"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                [2] = false  -- The second argument, set to false as in your original script
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Left Leg" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.GoldenHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Golden",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To God's Hand Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "God's Hand" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "God's Hand Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end

        _G.AntiRagdoll = Value
while _G.AntiRagdoll do
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == true then
repeat task.wait()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = true
end
until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == false
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = false
end
end
end
task.wait()
end
	end
