-- Global flag to control loop
_G.AutoSlapRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players (50+ Killstreak Users Only)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.AutoSlapRunning = state

        -- Check if player has Default glove
        local function hasDefaultGlove()
            local leaderstats = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Default" then
                    return true
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        -- Find player with 50 or more numbers in their nametag
        local function findPlayerWith50Plus()
            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                    local head = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if head then
                        local nametag = head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
                        if nametag then
                            local labels = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels")
                            if labels then
                                local topLabel = labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
                                if topLabel and topLabel:IsA("TextLabel") and topLabel.Text then
                                    -- Extract all numbers from the text
                                    local numbers = string.match(topLabel.Text, "%d+")
                                    if numbers then
                                        local numberValue = tonumber(numbers)
                                        if numberValue and numberValue >= 50 then
                                            print("Found player with " .. numberValue .. " numbers: " .. player.Name)
                                            return player
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            print("No player found with 50+ numbers in nametag")
            return nil
        end

        -- Teleport to player with 50+ numbers
        local function teleportToTargetPlayer()
            local targetPlayer = findPlayerWith50Plus()
            if targetPlayer then
                local char = targetPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localChar = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    local localHRP = localChar and localChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        print("Teleported to player: " .. targetPlayer.Name)
                        return true
                    else
                        print("Local player HRP not found")
                    end
                else
                    print("Target player character or HRP not found")
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        -- Fire remote "b" on all players
        local function fireRemoteForAllPlayers()
            local remote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("b")
            if not remote then
                print("Remote 'b' not found in ReplicatedStorage")
                return
            end
            
            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        local success, error = pcall(function()
                            remote:FireServer(rightArm)
                        end)
                        if not success then
                            warn("Failed to fire remote for player " .. player.Name .. ": " .. error)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoSlapLoop()
            -- Check for Default glove
            if not hasDefaultGlove() then
                print("Error: Equip Default glove first!")
                _G.AutoSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.AutoSlapRunning do
                -- Re-check glove every loop iteration
                if not hasDefaultGlove() then
                    print("Default glove not equipped! Stopping...")
                    _G.AutoSlapRunning = false
                    break
                end
                
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                
                -- Try to teleport to player with 50+ numbers
                local teleported = teleportToTargetPlayer()
                
                -- Fire remote on all players
                fireRemoteForAllPlayers()
                
                -- If no player with 50+ numbers found, wait a bit longer before checking again
                if not teleported then
                    task.wait(2)
                end
            end
        end

        if state then
            print("Auto Slap started - checking for Default glove...")
            if hasDefaultGlove() then
                print("Default glove equipped - looking for players with 50+ numbers in nametag")
                coroutine.wrap(runAutoSlapLoop)()
            else
                print("Error: Please equip Default glove first!")
                _G.AutoSlapRunning = false
            end
        else
            _G.AutoSlapRunning = false

        end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Trap",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- ===== VARIABLES =====
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

-- Timer variables
local isSpawningBricks = false
local brickSpawnStarted = false
local brickSpawnStopped = false
local brickSpawnFinished = false
local brickStartTime = nil
local brickElapsedTime = 0
local totalTimeNeeded = 25 * 60 -- 25 minutes in seconds (1500 seconds)
local savedStoppedTime = nil

-- Display variables for Trap Status
local currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto brick..."
local currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
local currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
local currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"

-- Brick counting variables
local totalBricksDropped = 0
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local ownBrickMasterBadge = false
local isBrickGloveEquipped = false
local brickSpawnLoop = nil

-- Badge display variables
local badgeStatusText = "Loading..."

-- Brick Master Badge ID
local BRICK_MASTER_BADGE_ID = 2127567042

-- Function to check if Brick glove is equipped
local function checkBrickGlove()
    local character = player.Character
    if character then
        local brickTool = character:FindFirstChild("Brick")
        if brickTool then
            isBrickGloveEquipped = true
            return true
        end
    end
    isBrickGloveEquipped = false
    return false
end

-- Function to check if Brick Master badge is owned
local function checkBrickMasterBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == BRICK_MASTER_BADGE_ID then
                    ownBrickMasterBadge = true
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    ownBrickMasterBadge = false
    return false
end

-- Function to update badge status text
local function updateBadgeStatusText()
    local badgeStatus = ownBrickMasterBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No"
    badgeStatusText = string.format([[
Owns Brick Master Badge: %s
Brick Master Badge Awards Glove: Trap Glove
]],
    badgeStatus
)
    return badgeStatusText
end

-- Function to format time EXACTLY LIKE MEGAROCK (Hours:Minutes:Seconds:Milliseconds)
local function formatTime(seconds, milliseconds)
    local hours = math.floor(seconds / 3600)
    local minutes = math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60)
    local secs = math.floor(seconds % 60)
    local ms = math.floor(milliseconds or 0)
    return string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d:%03d", hours, minutes, secs, ms)
end

-- Function to get brick count from UI
local function getBrickCountFromUI()
    local success, result = pcall(function()
        local playerGui = player.PlayerGui
        local brickCount = playerGui:FindFirstChild("BRICKCOUNT")
        if brickCount then
            local imageLabel = brickCount:FindFirstChild("ImageLabel")
            if imageLabel then
                local textLabel = imageLabel:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                if textLabel then
                    return tonumber(textLabel.Text) or 0
                end
            end
        end
        return 0
    end)
    if not success then
        return 0
    end
    return result
end

-- Function to update trap status display
local function updateTrapDisplay()
    -- Update status texts based on current state (SAME LOGIC AS MEGAROCK)
    if brickSpawnFinished then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Finished!"
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
        currentTimeStopped = "N/A"
        currentTimeFinished = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
    elseif brickSpawnStopped then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Stopped"
        local elapsedMs = (brickElapsedTime - math.floor(brickElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(brickElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = formatTime(brickElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif brickSpawnStarted then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Auto bricks started..."
        local elapsedMs = (brickElapsedTime - math.floor(brickElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(brickElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif not isSpawningBricks then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto brick..."
        currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    end
    
    -- Get current values
    local uiBrickCount = getBrickCountFromUI()
    local brickGloveStatus = isBrickGloveEquipped and "Yes" or "No"
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    
    -- Build status text (SAME FORMAT AS MEGAROCK)
    local statusText = string.format([[
Auto Spawn Bricks Time Waiting: %s
Auto Spawn Bricks Time Started: %s
Auto Spawn Bricks Time Stopped: %s
Auto Spawn Bricks Time Finished: %s
Total Time Need: %s
Total Bricks Dropped At Top: %d
Total Dropped Bricks: %d
Brick Glove Equipped: %s
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    currentTimeWaiting,
    currentTimeStarted,
    currentTimeStopped,
    currentTimeFinished,
    formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0),
    uiBrickCount,
    totalBricksDropped,
    brickGloveStatus,
    antiAfkStatus
    )
    
    return statusText
end

-- Create the TWO paragraphs
local TrapStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Trap Farm Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- ===== LOOP 1: TRAP STATUS UPDATE (0.01 SECONDS - LIKE MEGAROCK) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local startTime = tick()
        
        -- Update timer if running
        if brickSpawnStarted and not brickSpawnFinished and not brickSpawnStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            brickElapsedTime = currentTime - brickStartTime
        end
        
        -- Update glove status
        checkBrickGlove()
        
        -- Update the trap status paragraph
        local statusText = updateTrapDisplay()
        pcall(function()
            TrapStatusParagraph:Set(statusText)
        end)
        
        -- Maintain exactly 0.01 seconds like MEGAROCK
        local elapsed = tick() - startTime
        local waitTime = math.max(0.005, 0.01 - elapsed)
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 2: TIMER UPDATE (every frame for accuracy - LIKE MEGAROCK) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        if brickSpawnStarted and not brickSpawnFinished and not brickSpawnStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            brickElapsedTime = currentTime - brickStartTime
        end
        task.wait() -- Every frame for precise timing
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 3: BADGE STATUS UPDATE (5 SECONDS - SLOW) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        -- Check badge status
        checkBrickMasterBadge()
        
        -- Update badge status text
        local badgeText = updateBadgeStatusText()
        pcall(function()
            BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(badgeText)
        end)
        
        task.wait(5) -- Update every 5 seconds (badges don't change often)
    end
end)

-- Function to spawn bricks
local function startBrickSpawning()
    if brickSpawnLoop then
        task.cancel(brickSpawnLoop)
    end
    
    brickSpawnLoop = task.spawn(function()
        while isSpawningBricks and not brickSpawnFinished do
            pcall(function()
                -- Check if Brick glove is equipped and player has entered
                if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Brick" then
                    local char = player.Character
                    if char and char:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                        
                        -- Teleport to position
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if hrp then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(17895, -24, -3533)
                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end
                        
                        -- Fire remote to spawn brick
                        local lbrick = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("lbrick")
                        if lbrick then
                            lbrick:FireServer()
                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end
                        
                        -- Update UI brick count
                        pcall(function()
                            local playerGui = player.PlayerGui
                            local brickCount = playerGui:FindFirstChild("BRICKCOUNT")
                            if brickCount then
                                local imageLabel = brickCount:FindFirstChild("ImageLabel")
                                if imageLabel then
                                    local textLabel = imageLabel:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                                    if textLabel then
                                        local currentCount = tonumber(textLabel.Text) or 0
                                        textLabel.Text = tostring(currentCount + 1)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        
                        -- Add to dropped bricks counter
                        totalBricksDropped = totalBricksDropped + 1
                    end
                end
            end)
            task.wait(1.5) -- Wait between spawns
        end
    end)
end

-- ===== AUTO SPAWN BRICKS TOGGLE =====
local autoSpawnEnabled = false

local autoSpawnToggle = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Spawn Bricks",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoSpawnEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Brick glove is equipped and player has entered
            if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Brick" then
                local char = player.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                    
                    -- Reset and start timer (LIKE MEGAROCK)
                    isSpawningBricks = true
                    brickSpawnStarted = true
                    brickSpawnStopped = false
                    brickSpawnFinished = false
                    brickStartTime = tick()
                    brickElapsedTime = 0
                    savedStoppedTime = nil
                    totalBricksDropped = 0
                    
                    -- Start spawning
                    startBrickSpawning()
                    
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Auto Spawn Bricks",
                        Content = "Started! Will run for 25 minutes",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                else
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Brick/Enter Arena",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                    autoSpawnToggle:Set(false)
                    autoSpawnEnabled = false
                end
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Brick/Enter Arena",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoSpawnToggle:Set(false)
                autoSpawnEnabled = false
            end
        else
            -- Stop spawning (LIKE MEGAROCK)
            if brickSpawnLoop then
                task.cancel(brickSpawnLoop)
                brickSpawnLoop = nil
            end
            isSpawningBricks = false
            brickSpawnStopped = true
            brickSpawnStarted = false
            savedStoppedTime = brickElapsedTime
            
        end
    end
})

-- ===== ANTI AFK TOGGLE =====
AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

-- Initial updates
checkBrickGlove()
checkBrickMasterBadge()

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Hybrid",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Rage" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Leg"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                [2] = false  -- The second argument, set to false as in your original script
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Left Leg" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.GRRRR:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Rage",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Slapple",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Collect Slapples",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        BringSlapples = Value
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while BringSlapples do
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if not player then task.wait(0.1) continue end
                
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                if not character:FindFirstChild("entered") then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local slapplesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
                    and workspace.Arena:FindFirstChild("island5")
                    and workspace.Arena.island5:FindFirstChild("Slapples")
                
                if not slapplesFolder then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                for _, slapple in pairs(slapplesFolder:GetChildren()) do
                    if slapple:IsA("Model") and (slapple.Name == "Slapple" or slapple.Name == "GoldenSlapple") then
                        pcall(function()
                            -- Get the Glove part
                            local glove = slapple:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                            if glove then
                                -- Move the Glove DIRECTLY into the player's HRP (0 studs away)
                                glove.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                            else
                                -- If no Glove, move the whole model into the player
                                slapple:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(hrp.CFrame)
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                end
                
                task.wait(0.01) -- Run every 0.1 seconds
            end
        end)
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Disarm",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

    -- Global flag to control loop
_G.DisarmSlapRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players (Reaper)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.DisarmSlapRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player (not self)
        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            else
                warn("Not enough players to teleport.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire ReaperHit on all players
        local function fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("ReaperHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoDisarmSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Reaper") then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Disarm glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.DisarmSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoDisarmSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto Reaper Slap Aura",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Reaper" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Arm"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.ReaperHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Reaper",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Rattlebones",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

local CandyCornCollector = "Teleport" -- Default fallback
local AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
local AutoServerhopCandyCorns = false

Tab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Choose Option To Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Default = "Teleport",
    Options = {"Teleport", "Bring"},
    Callback = function(Value)
        CandyCornCollector = Value
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoCollectCandyCorns = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if player already has the badge
            if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Already Have Badge",
                    Content = "You already have Necromancer glove badge! The farm will not work.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7734059095",
                    Time = 5
                })
                AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                return
            end
            
            if CandyCornCollector == "Teleport" then
                -- Auto Teleport to Candy Corns (BaseParts)
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        -- Check for badge again in case they got it during farming
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                                Name = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Image = "rbxassetid://7734059095",
                                Time = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            break
                        end
                        
                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local foundCandyCorn = false
                            
                            -- Search for BaseParts in CandyCorns folder
                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end
                                
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    foundCandyCorn = true
                                    -- Teleport to the BasePart
                                    character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(part.Position + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0))
                                    task.wait(0.2) -- Small delay between teleports
                                    break -- Focus on one at a time
                                end
                            end
                            
                            if not foundCandyCorn then
                                task.wait(0.5) -- Wait if no candy corns found
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
            elseif CandyCornCollector == "Bring" then
                -- Auto Bring Candy Corns (BaseParts) to player - directly to touch
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        -- Check for badge again in case they got it during farming
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                                Name = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Image = "rbxassetid://7734059095",
                                Time = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            break
                        end
                        
                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local humanoidRootPart = character.HumanoidRootPart
                            
                            -- Bring all BaseParts in CandyCorns folder directly to player
                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end
                                
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    -- Move the BasePart directly to player's position (touching)
                                    part.CFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end
})

end

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Tycoon",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- ===== VARIABLES =====
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

-- Timer variables
local isAutoPlating = false
local plateStarted = false
local plateStopped = false
local plateFinished = false
local plateStartTime = nil
local plateElapsedTime = 0
local totalTimeNeeded = 600 -- 600 seconds (10 minutes)
local savedStoppedTime = nil

-- Display variables for Plate Status
local currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto plate..."
local currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
local currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
local currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"

-- Counting variables
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local ownPlateMasterBadge = false
local autoPlateLoop = nil

-- Badge display variables
local badgeStatusText = "Loading..."

-- Plate Master Badge ID
local PLATE_MASTER_BADGE_ID = 2129212145

-- Function to check total players in server
local function getTotalPlayers()
    return #game.Players:GetPlayers()
end

-- Function to check if player has entered arena
local function hasEntered()
    local char = player.Character
    if char then
        return char:FindFirstChild("entered") ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to get total time shows at top (from PlateIndicator)
local function getTotalTimeShowsAtTop()
    local success, result = pcall(function()
        local playerGui = player.PlayerGui
        local plateIndicator = playerGui:FindFirstChild("PlateIndicator")
        if plateIndicator then
            local textLabel = plateIndicator:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
            if textLabel and textLabel:IsA("TextLabel") then
                local text = textLabel.Text
                -- Extract only the number from text like "Plate Counter: 5"
                local number = tonumber(text:match("%d+"))
                return number or 0
            end
        end
        return 0
    end)
    if not success then
        return 0
    end
    return result
end

-- Function to check if Plate Master badge is owned
local function checkPlateMasterBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == PLATE_MASTER_BADGE_ID then
                    ownPlateMasterBadge = true
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    ownPlateMasterBadge = false
    return false
end

-- Function to update badge status text
local function updateBadgeStatusText()
    local badgeStatus = ownPlateMasterBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No"
    badgeStatusText = string.format([[
Owns Plate Master Badge: %s
Plate Master Badge Awards Glove: Tycoon Glove
]],
    badgeStatus
)
    return badgeStatusText
end

-- Function to format time EXACTLY LIKE MEGAROCK (Hours:Minutes:Seconds:Milliseconds)
local function formatTime(seconds, milliseconds)
    local hours = math.floor(seconds / 3600)
    local minutes = math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60)
    local secs = math.floor(seconds % 60)
    local ms = math.floor(milliseconds or 0)
    return string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d:%03d", hours, minutes, secs, ms)
end

-- Function to update plate status display
local function updatePlateDisplay()
    local totalPlayers = getTotalPlayers()
    local requiredPlayers = 7
    local playerCountStatus = (totalPlayers >= requiredPlayers) and totalPlayers .. "/" .. requiredPlayers or totalPlayers .. "/" .. requiredPlayers
    
    if plateFinished then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Finished!"
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
        currentTimeStopped = "N/A"
        currentTimeFinished = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
    elseif plateStopped then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Stopped"
        local elapsedMs = (plateElapsedTime - math.floor(plateElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(plateElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = formatTime(plateElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif plateStarted then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Auto plate started..."
        local elapsedMs = (plateElapsedTime - math.floor(plateElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(plateElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif not isAutoPlating then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto plate..."
        currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    end
    
    local totalTimeShowsAtTop = getTotalTimeShowsAtTop()
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Auto Plate Time Waiting: %s
Auto Plate Time Started: %s
Auto Plate Time Stopped: %s
Auto Plate Time Finished: %s
Total Time Need: %s
Total Time Shows At Top: %d
Total Players In Server: %s
Total Required Players In Server: 7
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    currentTimeWaiting,
    currentTimeStarted,
    currentTimeStopped,
    currentTimeFinished,
    formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0),
    totalTimeShowsAtTop,
    playerCountStatus,
    antiAfkStatus
    )
    
    return statusText
end

-- Create the TWO paragraphs
local PlateStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Auto Plate Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- ===== LOOP 1: PLATE STATUS UPDATE (0.01 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local startTime = tick()
        
        if plateStarted and not plateFinished and not plateStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            plateElapsedTime = currentTime - plateStartTime
        end
        
        local statusText = updatePlateDisplay()
        pcall(function()
            PlateStatusParagraph:Set(statusText)
        end)
        
        local elapsed = tick() - startTime
        local waitTime = math.max(0.005, 0.01 - elapsed)
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 2: TIMER UPDATE (every frame for accuracy) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        if plateStarted and not plateFinished and not plateStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            plateElapsedTime = currentTime - plateStartTime
            
            if plateElapsedTime >= totalTimeNeeded then
                plateFinished = true
                isAutoPlating = false
                plateStarted = false
                
                pcall(function()
                    AutoTycoon:Set(false)
                end)
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 3: BADGE STATUS UPDATE (5 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        checkPlateMasterBadge()
        local badgeText = updateBadgeStatusText()
        pcall(function()
            BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(badgeText)
        end)
        task.wait(2)
    end
end)

-- ===== AUTO TELEPORT TO PLATE TOGGLE =====
_G.AutoTpPlate = false

AutoTycoon = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Plate",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoTpPlate = Value
        
        if Value then
            if hasEntered() and getTotalPlayers() >= 7 then
                isAutoPlating = true
                plateStarted = true
                plateStopped = false
                plateFinished = false
                plateStartTime = tick()
                plateElapsedTime = 0
                savedStoppedTime = nil
                
                if autoPlateLoop then
                    task.cancel(autoPlateLoop)
                end
                
                autoPlateLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while _G.AutoTpPlate and isAutoPlating and not plateFinished do
                        -- Check conditions
                        if not hasEntered() or getTotalPlayers() < 7 then
                            -- Conditions failed - stop the toggle
                            if getTotalPlayers() < 7 then
                                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                                    Name = "Auto Plate",
                                    Content = "Not enough players! Need 7+ players.",
                                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                                    Time = 3
                                })
                            elseif not hasEntered() then
                                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                                    Name = "Auto Plate",
                                    Content = "You need to enter the arena!",
                                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                                    Time = 3
                                })
                            end
                            _G.AutoTpPlate = false
                            AutoTycoon:Set(false)
                            isAutoPlating = false
                            plateStopped = true
                            plateStarted = false
                            break
                        end
                        
                        -- Teleport to plate
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = player.Character
                            if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                local plate = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena") and workspace.Arena:FindFirstChild("Plate")
                                if plate and plate:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = plate.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
                
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Auto Plate",
                    Content = "Started! Will run for 10 minutes",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
            else
                local errorMsg = ""
                if not hasEntered() then
                    errorMsg = "You Need Enter Arena"
                elseif getTotalPlayers() < 7 then
                    errorMsg = "7+ People In Server Required (Current: " .. getTotalPlayers() .. ")"
                end
                
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                task.wait(0.05)
                AutoTycoon:Set(false)
                _G.AutoTpPlate = false
            end
        else
            if autoPlateLoop then
                task.cancel(autoPlateLoop)
                autoPlateLoop = nil
            end
            isAutoPlating = false
            plateStopped = true
            plateStarted = false
            savedStoppedTime = plateElapsedTime
            
        end
    end    
})

    Name = "Anti Afk",

    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

checkPlateMasterBadge()
BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(updateBadgeStatusText())
PlateStatusParagraph:Set(updatePlateDisplay())

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Bring Bus",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value) 
        Giftfarm = Value
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while Giftfarm do
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if not player then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                -- Find BusModel
                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "BusModel" then
                        pcall(function()
                            -- Method 1: Teleport the bus to the player (brings bus to you)
                            local busPrimaryPart = v:FindFirstChild("PrimaryPart") or v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or v:FindFirstChild("RootPart")
                            
                            if busPrimaryPart then
                                -- Move bus to player's position
                                busPrimaryPart.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                            else
                                -- If no primary part, move the whole model
                                local modelParts = {}
                                for _, part in pairs(v:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                        table.insert(modelParts, part)
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                -- Move each part to player
                                for _, part in pairs(modelParts) do
                                    part.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                            
                            -- Alternative: Move player to bus (if you want player to go to bus)
                            -- hrp.CFrame = v:GetPivot() + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                        end)
                    end
                end
                
                task.wait(0.05) -- Faster than original for better collection
            end
        end)
    end
})

        while _G.Glitchfarm do
            -- Ensure the player has the "Error" glove equipped
            local glove = game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove
            if glove and glove.Value == "Error" then
                -- Check if either "JetOrb" or "PhaseOrb" exists in the workspace

                -- If orbs are found, fire the Errorhit event

                if phaseOrb then
                    game.ReplicatedStorage.Errorhit:FireServer(phaseOrb)
                end
else
                -- Notify the player to equip the "Error" glove if they don't have it
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Error",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
            end
            
            -- Wait briefly before checking again to reduce load
            task.wait(1)  -- Adjust wait time as needed for performance
        end
    end
end
})

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Elude",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To ? Place + Auto TP To Glove",
    Callback = function()
local targetPlaceId = 11828384869
local targetPosition = Vector3.new(-503, 19, -179)
local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

-- Check if this is the first execution or a re-execution
local isReExecution = false

-- Function to teleport to position
local function teleportToPosition()
    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
        character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPosition)
        print("Teleported to target position!")
    end
end

-- Function to set up teleport monitoring
local function setupTeleportMonitor()
    local connection
    connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
        if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
            -- Save the script to re-execute after teleport
            local teleportScript = [[
                wait(2) -- Wait for character to load
                local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(-503, 19, -179))
                    print("Auto-executed teleport after arrival!")
                end
            ]]
            
            -- Use syn.queue_on_teleport or queue_on_teleport depending on executor
            if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                syn.queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
            else
                queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    return connection
end

-- Main execution logic
if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
    -- We're in the target place
    if isReExecution then
        print("Re-execution detected - performing final teleport")
        teleportToPosition()
        print("Auto-execution complete. Script will not run again automatically.")
    else
        -- First execution in target place
        print("First execution in target place - teleporting")
        teleportToPosition()
        
        -- Set up for potential future teleports
        setupTeleportMonitor()
    end
else
    -- We're not in the target place, teleport to the game
    print("Teleporting to target game...")
    local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
    
    local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
    local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
        TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
    end)
    
    if not success then
        print("Teleport failed:", errorMsg)
        if connection then
            connection:Disconnect()
        end
    end
end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "RNG",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Global flag to control loop
_G.DiceSlapRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.DiceSlapRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player (not self)
        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            else
                warn("Not enough players to teleport.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire DiceHit on all players
        local function fireDiceHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("DiceHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoDiceSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Dice") then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Dice glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.DiceSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.DiceSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireDiceHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoDiceSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.DiceSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto Dice Slap Aura",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Dice" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Head"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character.Head
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Head" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.DiceHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Dice",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "fish",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- ===== VARIABLES =====
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

-- Timer variables
local isAutoFishing = false
local fishStarted = false
local fishStopped = false
local fishFinished = false
local fishStartTime = nil
local fishElapsedTime = 0
local totalTimeNeeded = 60 * 60 -- 1 hour in seconds (3600 seconds)
local savedStoppedTime = nil

-- Display variables for Fish Status
local currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto fish..."
local currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
local currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
local currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"

-- Variables
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local ownDeepSlumberBadge = false
local autoFishLoop = nil
local autoFishEnabled = false
local remoteFired = false
local isFirstLoad = true -- Prevent initial trigger

-- Badge display variables
local badgeStatusText = "Loading..."

-- DEEP SLUMBER Badge ID
local DEEP_SLUMBER_BADGE_ID = 2130032297

-- Function to check if player's model has "zzz" attribute (exists when sleeping)
local function hasZZZAttribute()
    local char = player.Character
    if char then
        local zzzValue = char:GetAttribute("zzz")
        return zzzValue ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if player has entered arena
local function hasEntered()
    local char = player.Character
    if char then
        return char:FindFirstChild("entered") ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if ZZZZZZZ glove is equipped
local function hasZZZZZZZGlove()
    if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
        return player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "ZZZZZZZ"
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if DEEP SLUMBER badge is owned
local function checkDeepSlumberBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == DEEP_SLUMBER_BADGE_ID then
                    ownDeepSlumberBadge = true
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    ownDeepSlumberBadge = false
    return false
end

-- Function to update badge status text
local function updateBadgeStatusText()
    local badgeStatus = ownDeepSlumberBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No"
    badgeStatusText = string.format([[
Owns DEEP SLUMBER Badge: %s
DEEP SLUMBER Badge Awards Glove: fish Glove
]],
    badgeStatus
)
    return badgeStatusText
end

-- Function to format time (Hours:Minutes:Seconds:Milliseconds)
local function formatTime(seconds, milliseconds)
    local hours = math.floor(seconds / 3600)
    local minutes = math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60)
    local secs = math.floor(seconds % 60)
    local ms = math.floor(milliseconds or 0)
    return string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d:%03d", hours, minutes, secs, ms)
end

-- Function to update fish status display
local function updateFishDisplay()
    if fishFinished then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Finished!"
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
        currentTimeStopped = "N/A"
        currentTimeFinished = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
    elseif fishStopped then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Stopped"
        local elapsedMs = (fishElapsedTime - math.floor(fishElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(fishElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = formatTime(fishElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif fishStarted then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Auto fish started..."
        local elapsedMs = (fishElapsedTime - math.floor(fishElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(fishElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif not isAutoFishing then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto fish..."
        currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    end
    
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Auto fish Farm Time Waiting: %s
Auto fish Farm Time Started: %s
Auto fish Farm Time Stopped: %s
Auto fish Farm Time Finished: %s
Total Time Need: %s
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    currentTimeWaiting,
    currentTimeStarted,
    currentTimeStopped,
    currentTimeFinished,
    formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0),
    antiAfkStatus
    )
    
    return statusText
end

-- Create the TWO paragraphs
local FishStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Auto Fish Farm Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- ===== LOOP 1: FISH STATUS UPDATE (0.01 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local startTime = tick()
        
        if fishStarted and not fishFinished and not fishStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            fishElapsedTime = currentTime - fishStartTime
        end
        
        local statusText = updateFishDisplay()
        pcall(function()
            FishStatusParagraph:Set(statusText)
        end)
        
        local elapsed = tick() - startTime
        local waitTime = math.max(0.005, 0.01 - elapsed)
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 2: TIMER UPDATE (every frame for accuracy) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        if fishStarted and not fishFinished and not fishStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            fishElapsedTime = currentTime - fishStartTime
            
            if fishElapsedTime >= totalTimeNeeded then
                fishFinished = true
                isAutoFishing = false
                fishStarted = false
                
                pcall(function()
                    AutoFish:Set(false)
                end)
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 3: BADGE STATUS UPDATE (5 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        checkDeepSlumberBadge()
        local badgeText = updateBadgeStatusText()
        pcall(function()
            BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(badgeText)
        end)
        task.wait(5)
    end
end)

-- Function to fire ZZZZZZZSleep remote
local function fireSleepRemote()
    pcall(function()
        local sleepRemote = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("ZZZZZZZSleep")
        if sleepRemote then
            sleepRemote:FireServer()
            print("🔥 Sleep remote fired!")
        end
    end)
end

-- ===== AUTO GET FISH GLOVE TOGGLE =====
AutoFish = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Get fish Glove",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        -- Skip if this is the first load/initial trigger
        if isFirstLoad then
            isFirstLoad = false
            return
        end
        
        if Value then
            -- Check conditions before starting
            if not hasZZZZZZZGlove() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip ZZZZZZZ Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                AutoFish:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            if not hasEntered() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "You need to enter the arena!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                AutoFish:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            -- Reset remote fired flag
            remoteFired = false
            
            -- Reset and start timer
            isAutoFishing = true
            fishStarted = true
            fishStopped = false
            fishFinished = false
            fishStartTime = tick()
            fishElapsedTime = 0
            savedStoppedTime = nil
            autoFishEnabled = true
            
            -- DO TELEPORT ONCE
            local char = player.Character
            if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-17926, 60, 3531)
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
            
            -- USE REMOTE ONCE (if awake / no zzz attribute)
            if not hasZZZAttribute() then
                fireSleepRemote()
                remoteFired = true
            end
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Fish",
                Content = "Started! Teleported and used remote.",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            -- DISABLE TOGGLE
            autoFishEnabled = false
            
            -- Stop the loop if any
            if autoFishLoop then
                task.cancel(autoFishLoop)
                autoFishLoop = nil
            end
            
            -- Fire remote to WAKE UP (toggle off)
            fireSleepRemote()
            
            -- Reset timer states
            isAutoFishing = false
            fishStopped = true
            fishStarted = false
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Fish",
                Content = "Stopped! Time elapsed: " .. formatTime(fishElapsedTime, 0),
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end    
})

-- ===== ANTI AFK TOGGLE =====
AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

-- Initial updates
checkDeepSlumberBadge()
BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(updateBadgeStatusText())
FishStatusParagraph:Set(updateFishDisplay())

end

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Obby",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Obby's Status Counter"
})

-- ===== VARIABLES =====
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

-- Touch counting variables
local touchedPlayers = {} -- Table to track which players have touched
local totalPeopleTouched = 0
local totalPeopleNeeded = 10
local isTracking = false

-- Variables
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local ownUltrarockBadge = false
local isTrackingActive = false

-- Badge display variables
local badgeStatusText = "Loading..."

-- ULTRAROCK Badge ID
local ULTRAROCK_BADGE_ID = 2130463063

-- Valid gloves for tracking
local validGloves = {
    "Diamond",
    "MEGAROCK",
    "CUSTOM"
}

-- Function to check if player has valid glove
local function hasValidGlove()
    if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
        local currentGlove = player.leaderstats.Glove.Value
        for _, glove in ipairs(validGloves) do
            if currentGlove == glove then
                return true
            end
        end
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if player has entered arena
local function hasEntered()
    local char = player.Character
    if char then
        return char:FindFirstChild("entered") ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if player has rock
local function hasRock()
    local char = player.Character
    if char then
        return char:FindFirstChild("rock") ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if ULTRAROCK badge is owned
local function checkUltrarockBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == ULTRAROCK_BADGE_ID then
                    ownUltrarockBadge = true
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    ownUltrarockBadge = false
    return false
end

-- Function to update badge status text
local function updateBadgeStatusText()
    local badgeStatus = ownUltrarockBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No"
    badgeStatusText = string.format([[
Owns ULTRAROCK Badge: %s
ULTRAROCK Badge Awards Glove: Obby Glove
]],
    badgeStatus
)
    return badgeStatusText
end

-- Function to update tracking display
local function updateTrackingDisplay()
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Total People Touched You: %d/%d
Total People Need To Touch You: %d
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    totalPeopleTouched,
    totalPeopleNeeded,
    totalPeopleNeeded,
    antiAfkStatus
    )
    
    return statusText
end

-- Function to check for players touching the rock
local function startTouchTracking()
    isTrackingActive = true
    
    -- Track when players touch the rock
    local function onPartTouched(otherPart)
        if not isTracking then return end
        
        local character = otherPart.Parent
        if not character then return end
        
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        if not humanoid then return end
        
        local otherPlayer = game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(character)
        if not otherPlayer then return end
        
        -- Don't count yourself
        if otherPlayer == player then return end
        
        local playerName = otherPlayer.Name
        
        -- Check if this player hasn't touched before
        if not touchedPlayers[playerName] then
            touchedPlayers[playerName] = true
            totalPeopleTouched = totalPeopleTouched + 1
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "ULTRAROCK",
                Content = playerName .. " touched your rock! (" .. totalPeopleTouched .. "/" .. totalPeopleNeeded .. ")",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 2
            })
            
            -- Update display
            UltrarockStatusParagraph:Set(updateTrackingDisplay())
            
            -- Check if reached goal
            if totalPeopleTouched >= totalPeopleNeeded then
                isTracking = false
                
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "ULTRAROCK",
                    Content = "Goal reached! " .. totalPeopleTouched .. "/" .. totalPeopleNeeded .. " players touched you!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 5
                })
                
                -- Disable the toggle
                pcall(function()
                    UltrarockToggle:Set(false)
                end)
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- Wait for rock to appear
    local function waitForRock()
        while isTracking do
            local char = player.Character
            if char then
                local rock = char:FindFirstChild("rock")
                if rock and rock:IsA("BasePart") then
                    -- Connect touch event
                    rock.Touched:Connect(onPartTouched)
                    break
                end
            end
            task.wait(0.5)
        end
    end
    
    task.spawn(waitForRock)
end

-- Create the TWO paragraphs
local UltrarockStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("ULTRAROCK Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- ===== LOOP: STATUS UPDATE (every 0.5 seconds) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local statusText = updateTrackingDisplay()
        pcall(function()
            UltrarockStatusParagraph:Set(statusText)
        end)
        task.wait(0.5)
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP: BADGE STATUS UPDATE (5 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        checkUltrarockBadge()
        local badgeText = updateBadgeStatusText()
        pcall(function()
            BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(badgeText)
        end)
        task.wait(5)
    end
end)

-- ===== ULTRAROCK TRACKING TOGGLE =====
local toggleEnabled = false

UltrarockToggle = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "ULTRAROCK Badge Tracker",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            -- Check conditions
            if not hasValidGlove() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Diamond, MEGAROCK or CUSTOM Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                UltrarockToggle:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            if not hasEntered() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "You need to enter the arena!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                UltrarockToggle:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            if not hasRock() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "You need to have rock form! Use MEGAROCK ability first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                UltrarockToggle:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            -- Reset tracking
            touchedPlayers = {}
            totalPeopleTouched = 0
            isTracking = true
            
            -- Start touch tracking
            startTouchTracking()
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "ULTRAROCK",
                Content = "Tracking started! Need " .. totalPeopleNeeded .. " different players to touch your rock.",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 4
            })
        else
            -- Stop tracking
            isTracking = false
            isTrackingActive = false
            
        end
    end
})

-- ===== ANTI AFK TOGGLE =====
AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

-- Initial updates
checkUltrarockBadge()
BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(updateBadgeStatusText())
UltrarockStatusParagraph:Set(updateTrackingDisplay())

-- Timer variables

local voodooStarted = false
local voodooStopped = false
local voodooFinished = false
local voodooStartTime = nil
local voodooElapsedTime = 0
local totalTimeNeeded = 60 * 60 -- 1 hour in seconds (3600 seconds)
local savedStoppedTime = nil

-- Display variables for Voodoo Status
local currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto voodoo..."
local currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"

local currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"

local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local ownInsanityBadge = false
local autoVoodooLoop = nil

-- Badge display variables
local badgeStatusText = "Loading..."

-- Insanity Badge ID

-- Function to check if player has entered arena
local function hasEntered()

    if char then
        return char:FindFirstChild("entered") ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if Ghost glove is equipped
local function hasGhostGlove()
    if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
        return player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Ghost"
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if Insanity badge is owned
local function checkInsanityBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)

    local minutes = math.floor((seconds % 3600) / 60)
    local secs = math.floor(seconds % 60)
    local ms = math.floor(milliseconds or 0)
    return string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d:%03d", hours, minutes, secs, ms)

-- Function to fire Ghost invisibility remote

    end)

-- Function to update voodoo status display
local function updateVoodooDisplay()

        currentTimeWaiting = "Finished!"
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
        currentTimeStopped = "N/A"
        currentTimeFinished = formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0)
    elseif voodooStopped then
