        local elapsedMs = (voodooElapsedTime - math.floor(voodooElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(voodooElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = formatTime(voodooElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif voodooStarted then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Auto voodoo started..."
        local elapsedMs = (voodooElapsedTime - math.floor(voodooElapsedTime)) * 1000
        currentTimeStarted = formatTime(voodooElapsedTime, elapsedMs)
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    elseif not isAutoVoodoo then
        currentTimeWaiting = "Waiting for auto voodoo..."
        currentTimeStarted = "Not Started"
        currentTimeStopped = "Not Stopped"
        currentTimeFinished = "Not Finished"
    end
    
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Auto Voodoo Farm Time Waiting: %s
Auto Voodoo Farm Time Started: %s
Auto Voodoo Farm Time Stopped: %s
Auto Voodoo Farm Time Finished: %s
Total Time Need: %s
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    currentTimeWaiting,
    currentTimeStarted,
    currentTimeStopped,
    currentTimeFinished,
    formatTime(totalTimeNeeded, 0),
    antiAfkStatus
    )
    
    return statusText
end

-- Create the TWO paragraphs
local VoodooStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Auto Voodoo Farm Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- ===== LOOP 1: VOODOO STATUS UPDATE (0.01 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local startTime = tick()
        
        if voodooStarted and not voodooFinished and not voodooStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            voodooElapsedTime = currentTime - voodooStartTime
        end
        
        local statusText = updateVoodooDisplay()
        pcall(function()
            VoodooStatusParagraph:Set(statusText)
        end)
        
        local elapsed = tick() - startTime
        local waitTime = math.max(0.005, 0.01 - elapsed)
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 2: TIMER UPDATE (every frame for accuracy) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        if voodooStarted and not voodooFinished and not voodooStopped then
            local currentTime = tick()
            voodooElapsedTime = currentTime - voodooStartTime
            
            if voodooElapsedTime >= totalTimeNeeded then
                voodooFinished = true
                isAutoVoodoo = false
                voodooStarted = false
                
                pcall(function()
                    AutoVoodoo:Set(false)
                end)
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP 3: BADGE STATUS UPDATE (5 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        checkInsanityBadge()
        local badgeText = updateBadgeStatusText()
        pcall(function()
            BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(badgeText)
        end)
        task.wait(5)
    end
end)

-- ===== AUTO GET VOODOO GLOVE TOGGLE =====
AutoVoodoo = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Get Voodoo Glove",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            -- Check conditions before starting
            if not hasGhostGlove() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Ghost Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                AutoVoodoo:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            if not hasEntered() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "You need to enter the arena!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                AutoVoodoo:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            -- Reset and start timer
            isAutoVoodoo = true
            voodooStarted = true
            voodooStopped = false
            voodooFinished = false
            voodooStartTime = tick()
            voodooElapsedTime = 0
            savedStoppedTime = nil
            
            -- Start the voodoo loop
            if autoVoodooLoop then
                task.cancel(autoVoodooLoop)
                autoVoodooLoop = nil
            end
            
            autoVoodooLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while AutoVoodoo and isAutoVoodoo and not voodooFinished do
                    -- Check conditions every iteration
                    if not hasGhostGlove() then
                        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                            Name = "Auto Voodoo",
                            Content = "Ghost Glove unequipped! Stopping...",
                            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                            Time = 3
                        })
                        AutoVoodoo:Set(false)
                        break
                    end
                    
                    if not hasEntered() then
                        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                            Name = "Auto Voodoo",
                            Content = "Left arena! Stopping...",
                            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                            Time = 3
                        })
                        AutoVoodoo:Set(false)
                        break
                    end
                    
                    -- Teleport to position
                    local char = player.Character
                    if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(10001, -42, 10000)
                        task.wait(1)
                    end
                    
                    -- Fire remote
                    fireGhostRemote()
                    
                    -- Update timer
                    if voodooStarted and not voodooFinished then
                        local currentTime = tick()
                        voodooElapsedTime = currentTime - voodooStartTime
                        
                        if voodooElapsedTime >= totalTimeNeeded then
                            voodooFinished = true
                            isAutoVoodoo = false
                            voodooStarted = false
                            AutoVoodoo:Set(false)
                            break
                        end
                    end
                    
                    task.wait(1.5) -- Wait between attempts
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Voodoo",
                Content = "Started! Will run for 1 hour",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            -- DISABLE TOGGLE
            if autoVoodooLoop then
                task.cancel(autoVoodooLoop)
                autoVoodooLoop = nil
            end
            isAutoVoodoo = false
            voodooStopped = true
            voodooStarted = false
            savedStoppedTime = voodooElapsedTime
            
        end
    end    
})

-- ===== ANTI AFK TOGGLE =====
AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

-- Initial updates
checkInsanityBadge()
BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(updateBadgeStatusText())
VoodooStatusParagraph:Set(updateVoodooDisplay())

end

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Confusion Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Confusion" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Confusion Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Global flag to control loop
_G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap OVERKILL Players (Boomerang)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player with OVERKILL (not self)
        local function teleportToOverkillPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            local overkillPlayers = {}
            
            -- Find all players with OVERKILL
            for _, player in pairs(playerList) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" then
                        table.insert(overkillPlayers, player)
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if #overkillPlayers > 0 then
                local randomPlayer = overkillPlayers[math.random(1, #overkillPlayers)]
                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            else
                warn("No players with OVERKILL found.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire Snow hits on OVERKILL players only
        local function fireBoomerangHForOverkillPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" and player.Character then
                        local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                        if rightArm then
                            ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("BoomerangH"):FireServer(rightArm)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoBoomerangHOverkillLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Boomerang") then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Boomerang glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning do
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                teleportToOverkillPlayer()
                fireBoomerangHForOverkillPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoBoomerangHOverkillLoop)()
        else
            _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Boomerang Slap Aura (OVERKILL Players Only)",
    Callback = function()   
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Boomerang" then
            -- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            -- Start the infinite loop to fire for OVERKILL players only
            while true do
                -- Loop through each player in the game
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    -- Check if player has OVERKILL glove
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                        local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                        local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                        
                        -- Only target players with OVERKILL glove
                        if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
                            local args = {
                                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                            }

                            -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
                            ReplicatedStorage.BoomerangH:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end

                -- Wait 0.5 seconds before running the loop again
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "Equip Boomerang", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
        end
    end
})

end

Tab = Window:MakeTab({

Tab:AddButton({

-- ===== VARIABLES =====
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

-- Counter variables
local usedSelfKnockbackTimes = 0
local usedStunAbilityTimes = 0
local requiredSelfKnockback = 100
local requiredStunAbility = 50
local isAutoKinetic = false

-- Variables
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local ownKineticallyChargedBadge = false
local autoKineticLoop = nil

-- Badge display variables
local badgeStatusText = "Loading..."

-- Kinetically Charged Badge ID
local KINETICALLY_CHARGED_BADGE_ID = 2141386326

-- Function to check if player has entered arena
local function hasEntered()
    local char = player.Character
    if char then
        return char:FindFirstChild("entered") ~= nil
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if Stun glove is equipped
local function hasStunGlove()
    if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
        return player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Stun"
    end
    return false
end

-- Function to check if Kinetically Charged badge is owned
local function checkKineticallyChargedBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == KINETICALLY_CHARGED_BADGE_ID then
                    ownKineticallyChargedBadge = true
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    ownKineticallyChargedBadge = false
    return false
end

-- Function to update badge status text
local function updateBadgeStatusText()
    local badgeStatus = ownKineticallyChargedBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No"
    badgeStatusText = string.format([[
Owns Kinetically Charged Badge: %s
Kinetically Charged Badge Awards Glove: Kinetic Glove
]],
    badgeStatus
)
    return badgeStatusText
end

-- Function to update kinetic status display
local function updateKineticDisplay()
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    local selfKnockbackStatus = usedSelfKnockbackTimes .. "/" .. requiredSelfKnockback
    local stunAbilityStatus = usedStunAbilityTimes .. "/" .. requiredStunAbility
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Used Self Knockback Times: %s
Used Stun Ability Times: %s
Required Self Knockback Times: %d
Required Stun Ability Times: %d
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    selfKnockbackStatus,
    stunAbilityStatus,
    requiredSelfKnockback,
    requiredStunAbility,
    antiAfkStatus
    )
    
    return statusText
end

-- Create the TWO paragraphs
local KineticStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Auto Kinetic Farm Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- ===== LOOP: STATUS UPDATE =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local statusText = updateKineticDisplay()
        pcall(function()
            KineticStatusParagraph:Set(statusText)
        end)
        task.wait(0.5)
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP: BADGE STATUS UPDATE (5 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        checkKineticallyChargedBadge()
        local badgeText = updateBadgeStatusText()
        pcall(function()
            BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(badgeText)
        end)
        task.wait(5)
    end
end)

-- Function to fire SelfKnockback remote
local function fireSelfKnockback()
    pcall(function()
        local selfKnockback = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("SelfKnockback")
        if selfKnockback then
            selfKnockback:FireServer({["Force"] = 0, ["Direction"] = Vector3.new(0, 0.01, 0)})
            usedSelfKnockbackTimes = usedSelfKnockbackTimes + 1
        end
    end)
end

-- Function to fire StunR remote
local function fireStunR(stun)
    pcall(function()
        local stunR = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("StunR")
        if stunR and stun then
            stunR:FireServer(stun)
            usedStunAbilityTimes = usedStunAbilityTimes + 1
        end
    end)
end

-- ===== AUTO GET KINETIC GLOVE TOGGLE =====
AutoKinetic = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Get Kinetic Glove",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            -- Check conditions before starting
            if not hasStunGlove() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Stun Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                AutoKinetic:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            if not hasEntered() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "You need to enter the arena!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                AutoKinetic:Set(false)
                return
            end
            
            -- Reset counters
            usedSelfKnockbackTimes = 0
            usedStunAbilityTimes = 0
            
            -- Start the kinetic loop
            if autoKineticLoop then
                task.cancel(autoKineticLoop)
                autoKineticLoop = nil
            end
            
            autoKineticLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local char = player.Character
                local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                
                if not hrp then return end
                
                -- Save original position
                local OGL = hrp.CFrame
                
                -- Teleport to position
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10001, -42, 10000)
                task.wait(0.2)
                
                -- Fire self knockback 100 times
                for i = 1, requiredSelfKnockback do
                    if not AutoKinetic then break end
                    fireSelfKnockback()
                    task.wait(0.05)
                end
                
                task.wait(1.5)
                
                -- Main stun loop
                while AutoKinetic and isAutoKinetic do
                    -- Check conditions
                    if not hasStunGlove() then
                        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                            Name = "Auto Kinetic",
                            Content = "Stun Glove unequipped! Stopping...",
                            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                            Time = 3
                        })
                        AutoKinetic:Set(false)
                        break
                    end
                    
                    if not hasEntered() then
                        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                            Name = "Auto Kinetic",
                            Content = "Left arena! Stopping...",
                            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                            Time = 3
                        })
                        AutoKinetic:Set(false)
                        break
                    end
                    
                    -- Check if reached stun goal
                    if usedStunAbilityTimes >= requiredStunAbility then
                        AutoKinetic:Set(false)
                        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                            Name = "Success",
                            Content = "Kinetic Glove unlocked!",
                            Image = "rbxassetid://7733975185",
                            Time = 5
                        })
                        break
                    end
                    
                    -- Find valid random player
                    local players = game.Players:GetPlayers()
                    if #players >= 2 then
                        local targetPlayer = nil
                        local findAttempts = 0
                        
                        while not targetPlayer and findAttempts < 30 do
                            findAttempts = findAttempts + 1
                            local randomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)]
                            
                            if randomPlayer ~= player then
                                local targetChar = randomPlayer.Character
                                if targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                                    local targetHumanoid = targetChar:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                    if targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 then
                                        targetPlayer = randomPlayer
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end
                        
                        if targetPlayer then
                            char = player.Character
                            hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then break end
                            
                            -- Teleport to target
                            local targetChar = targetPlayer.Character
                            if targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                hrp.CFrame = targetChar.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -20, 0)
                                task.wait(0.25)
                            end
                            
                            -- Fire stun remote
                            local stun = char:FindFirstChild("Stun")
                            if stun then
                                fireStunR(stun)
                                
                                -- Show progress
                                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                                    Name = "Progress",
                                    Content = "Stun Ability [ " .. usedStunAbilityTimes .. " / " .. requiredStunAbility .. " ]",
                                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733975185",
                                    Time = 3
                                })
                            end
                            
                            -- Teleport back to position (10001, -42, 10000)
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10001, -42, 10000)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            
                            task.wait(12.3)
                        else
                            task.wait(2)
                        end
                    else
                        task.wait(2)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Kinetic",
                Content = "Started! Need " .. requiredSelfKnockback .. " self knockbacks and " .. requiredStunAbility .. " stuns",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 4
            })
        else
            -- DISABLE TOGGLE
            if autoKineticLoop then
                task.cancel(autoKineticLoop)
                autoKineticLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end    
})

-- ===== ANTI AFK TOGGLE =====
AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Someone Using Kinetic?",

        local found = false

            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Kinetic" then
                    found = true
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Kinetic glove.",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Kinetic glove",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Kinetic Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Kinetic" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Kinetic Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

AntiRagdoll = Tab:AddToggle({
	Name = "Anti Ragdoll",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AntiRagdoll = Value
while _G.AntiRagdoll do
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") then
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == true then
repeat task.wait()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = true
end
until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == false
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = false
end
end
end
task.wait()
end
	end    
})

end

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Reverse Slap Aura (Reverse Players Only)",
    Callback = function()   
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Reverse" then
            -- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            -- Start the infinite loop to fire for OVERKILL players only
            while true do
                -- Loop through each player in the game
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    -- Check if player has OVERKILL glove
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                        local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                        local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                        
                        -- Only target players with OVERKILL glove
                        if glove and glove.Value == "Reverse" and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
                            local args = {
                                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                            }

                            -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
                            ReplicatedStorage.ReverseHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end

                -- Wait 0.5 seconds before running the loop again
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "Equip Reverse", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
        end
    end
})

local AnswersSection = Tab:AddSection({ Name = "Answers" })

AnswersSection:AddParagraph("Note",
    "Make sure that you are in Limbo World first before using that button otherwise it will say that changed 0 and 0 so it wont really change because if u enter into Limbo World it will show that changed more than like greater than 0")

AnswersSection:AddButton({
    Name = "Set Correct/Incorrect Answers",
    Callback = function()
        local rightCount = 0
        local failCount = 0
        
        local rm = workspace:FindFirstChild("RepressedMemories")
        if not rm then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Not in RepressedMemories!",
                Time = 2
            })
            return
        end
        
        -- Search through all DialogChoice objects
        for _, obj in pairs(rm:GetDescendants()) do
            if obj:IsA("DialogChoice") and obj.UserDialog then
                local currentText = obj.UserDialog
                
                -- Check if it has a RightChoice Folder as child
                if obj:FindFirstChild("RightChoice") then
                    -- Add ✅ if not already present
                    if not string.find(currentText, "✅") then
                        obj.UserDialog = currentText .. " ✅"
                        rightCount = rightCount + 1
                    else
                        rightCount = rightCount + 1 -- Count as already has it
                    end
                end
                
                -- Check if it has a FailChoice Folder as child
                if obj:FindFirstChild("FailChoice") then
                    -- Add ❌ if not already present
                    if not string.find(currentText, "❌") then
                        obj.UserDialog = currentText .. " ❌"
                        failCount = failCount + 1
                    else
                        failCount = failCount + 1 -- Count as already has it
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Symbols Added",
            Content = "Added ✅ to " .. rightCount .. " correct answers\nAdded ❌ to " .. failCount .. " incorrect answers",
            Time = 4
        })
    end
})

    "Dance on top of the clone's head (by typing /e dance) if it says Simon says. Walk through the portal if it doesn't say Simon says")

    "Self-explanatory. Walk through the portal if it says Simon says. Jump off the map if it doesn't say Simon says")

SimonSection:AddParagraph("Simon says jump off the map to claim your reward",
    "Self-explanatory. Jump off the map if it says Simon says. Walk through the portal if it doesn't say Simon says")

SimonSection:AddParagraph("Simon says if the reward is what you seek, You must dance on top of the Right/Left staircase Crystal.",
    "Dance on top of the Crystals according to the NPC's Perspective by using the command (/e dance) in chat. If it says, (Left Crystal), You go and Dance on the Right Crystal (Its Left will be your Right and its Right will be your Left). Walk through the portal if it doesn't say Simon says")

SimonSection:AddParagraph("Simon says riddle me this and speak it out. What has four fingers and a thumb but isn't alive?",
    "Type (a glove) in chat.")

SimonSection:AddParagraph("Simon says riddle me this and speak it out. What has a bottom at the top?",
    "Type (a leg) in chat.")

-- Button 1: Teleport To NPC Head And Dance
SimonSection:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To NPC Head And Dance",
    Callback = function()
        -- Dance function inside this button
        local function startDance()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character
            if not character then return end
            
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            if not humanoid then return end
            
            local danceAnim = Instance.new("Animation")
            danceAnim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://507766756"
            
            local danceTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(danceAnim)
            if danceTrack then
                danceTrack:Play()
            end
        end
        
        -- Teleport function inside this button
        local function teleportTo(position)
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character
            if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(position)
            end
        end
        
        if not workspace:FindFirstChild("RepressedMemories") then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "RepressedMemories not found!",
                Time = 2
            })
            return
        end
        
        local npcHead = workspace.RepressedMemories:FindFirstChild("RepressedMemoriesNPC")
        if npcHead then
            npcHead = npcHead:FindFirstChild("Head")
        end
        
        if npcHead and npcHead:IsA("BasePart") then
            teleportTo(npcHead.Position)
            task.wait(0.1)
            startDance()
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Teleported",
                Content = "Teleported to NPC Head and dancing!",
                Time = 2
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "NPC Head not found!",
                Time = 2
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Button 2: Teleport To Portal
SimonSection:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Portal",
    Callback = function()
        local function teleportTo(position)
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        teleportTo(Vector3.new(18823, 3007, -225))

            Time = 2
        })
    end
})

                Time = 2

        teleportTo(Vector3.new(18666, 3019, -336))

            Time = 2

-- Button 5: Teleport To Top Right Crystal And Dance
SimonSection:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Top Right Crystal And Dance",
    Callback = function()
        local function startDance()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character
            if not character then return end
            
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            if not humanoid then return end
            
            local danceAnim = Instance.new("Animation")
            danceAnim.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://507766756"
            
            local danceTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(danceAnim)
            if danceTrack then
                danceTrack:Play()
            end
        end
        
        local function teleportTo(position)
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character
            if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(position)
            end
        end
        
        if not workspace:FindFirstChild("RepressedMemories") then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "RepressedMemories not found!",
                Time = 2
            })
            return
        end
        
        teleportTo(Vector3.new(18667, 3019, -117))
        task.wait(0.1)
        startDance()
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Teleported",
            Content = "Teleported to Top Right Crystal and dancing!",
            Time = 2
        })
    end
})

-- Button 6: Say "a glove" In Chat
SimonSection:AddButton({
    Name = 'Say "a glove" In Chat (Needs Chat Unlocked)',
    Callback = function()
        local function sendChatMessage(message)
            local textChatService = game:GetService("TextChatService")
            
            if textChatService and textChatService.TextChannels then
                local textChannel = textChatService.TextChannels:FindFirstChild("RBXGeneral")
                if textChannel and textChannel.SendAsync then  -- Fixed: removed the parentheses
                    textChannel:SendAsync(message)
                    return
                end
            end
            
            local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local chatEvent = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents")
            if chatEvent then
                local sendEvent = chatEvent:FindFirstChild("SayMessageRequest")
                if sendEvent then
                    sendEvent:FireServer(message, "All")
                    return
                end
            end
        end
        
        if not workspace:FindFirstChild("RepressedMemories") then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "RepressedMemories not found!",
                Time = 2
            })
            return
        end
        
        sendChatMessage("a glove")
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Message Sent",
            Content = 'Sent "a glove" to chat',
            Time = 2
        })
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To woah Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "woah" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "woah Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Berserk Charge",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility2s = Value
        
        if Value then
            print("Auto General Ability started - firing every 2 seconds")
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility2s and task.wait(2) do
                    local success, error = pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").BerserkCharge:FireServer()
                    end)
                    
                    if success then
                        print("Fired GeneralAbility remote")
                    else
                        warn("Failed to fire GeneralAbility:", error)
                    end
                end
            end)
        else

        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Reverse Slap Aura (Reverse Players Only)",
    Callback = function()   
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Reverse" then
            -- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            -- Start the infinite loop to fire for OVERKILL players only
            while true do
                -- Loop through each player in the game
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    -- Check if player has OVERKILL glove
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                        local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                        local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                        
                        -- Only target players with OVERKILL glove
                        if glove and glove.Value == "Reverse" and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
                            local args = {
                                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                            }

                            -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
                            ReplicatedStorage.ReverseHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end

                -- Wait 0.5 seconds before running the loop again
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "Equip Reverse", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Get Psycho Glove",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("RepressedMemoriesMap") ~= nil then
OGL = game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StartPsychoEvent.CFrame
OGL1 = game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StopPsychoEvent.CFrame
wait(5)
game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StartPsychoEvent.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
wait(5)
game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StartPsychoEvent.CFrame = OGL
wait(5)
game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StopPsychoEvent.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
wait(5)
game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StopPsychoEvent.CFrame = OGL1
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Be In Limbo World",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
  	end 
})

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Counter",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To ? Place + Auto Get Counter",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 11828384869
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        -- Function to execute the Counter script
        local function executeCounterScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetCounterExecuted then return end

            getgenv().AutoGetCounterExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == 11828384869 then
                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v)
                    end
                end

                local hrp = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1000, 1000, 1000)
                task.wait(0.6)
                hrp.Anchored = true

                local Time = 120
                while Time > 0 do
                    local msg = Instance.new("Message", workspace)
                    msg.Text = "Time left to receive: " .. Time
                    task.wait(1)
                    Time -= 1
                    msg:Destroy()
                end

                task.wait(1.5)

                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v)
                    end
                end
            else
                local places = {
                    11520107397, 9015014224, 6403373529, 124596094333302
                }

                for _, id in ipairs(places) do
                    if game.PlaceId == id then
                        while task.wait() do
                            game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(11828384869)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    -- Save the Counter script to re-execute after teleport
                    local counterScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        -- Execute Counter script after arriving
                        if game.PlaceId == 11828384869 then
                            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(v)
                                end
                            end

                            local hrp = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1000, 1000, 1000)
                            task.wait(0.6)
                            hrp.Anchored = true

                            local Time = 120
                            while Time > 0 do
                                local msg = Instance.new("Message", workspace)
                                msg.Text = "Time left to receive: " .. Time
                                task.wait(1)
                                Time -= 1
                                msg:Destroy()
                            end

                            task.wait(1.5)

                            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(v)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    -- Use syn.queue_on_teleport or queue_on_teleport depending on executor
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(counterScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(counterScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            -- We're already in the target place, execute Counter script directly
            print("Already in target place - executing Counter script")
            executeCounterScript()
        else
            -- We're not in the target place, teleport to the game
            print("Teleporting to target game...")
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            
            if not success then
                print("Teleport failed:", errorMsg)
                if connection then
                    connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Hammer",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Click On Toolbox",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(Value)
Toolboxfarm = Value
while Toolboxfarm do
if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Toolbox") then
for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.Name == "Toolbox" and v:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
fireclickdetector(v.ClickDetector, 0)
fireclickdetector(v.ClickDetector, 1)
                    end
                end
            end
task.wait()
end
	end    
})

                        Name = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Tycoon glove.",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Tycoon glove",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Reaper Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Reaper" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Reaper Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end

})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Reaper Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()   
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Reaper" then
            -- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            -- Loop through each player in the game and slap them once
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Arm"
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                    -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
                    local args = {
                        [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                    }

                    -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
                    ReplicatedStorage.ReaperHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                end
            end
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Reaper",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Click Tycoon",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(Value)
		_G.AutoTycoon = Value

		while _G.AutoTycoon do
			for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
				if string.find(v.Name, "ÅTycoon") then
					local clickPart = v:FindFirstChild("Click")
					if clickPart and clickPart:IsA("BasePart") then
						local detector = clickPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
						if detector then
							fireclickdetector(detector)
						end
					end
				end
			end
			task.wait()
		end
	end
})

end

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Use Track Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Start the loop
            getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility then
                    getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection:Disconnect()
                    return
                end
                
                -- Fire the remote every 13 seconds
                task.wait(13)
                if getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility then
                    pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
                        print("Fired GeneralAbility remote")
                    end)
                end
            end)
        else
            -- Stop the loop
            if getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection then
                getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

end

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Null",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Auto Teleport to Null Position + Get Null
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Null Zone Place + Get Null",
    Callback = function()
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
            -- Check if player has Pan glove equipped
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Pan" then
                -- Player has Pan equipped, teleport to position
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(18662, 2993, -298)
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Teleported!",
                        Content = "Pan user teleported to Null position",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 5
                    })
                end
            else
                -- Player doesn't have Pan equipped
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Pan glove first!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
            
        elseif currentPlaceId == 14422118326 then
            -- Already in Null Zone, get Null glove
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(5458, -189, 1854)
                wait(2)
                if workspace:FindFirstChild("Model") and workspace.Model:FindFirstChild("Handle") and workspace.Model.Handle:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                    fireclickdetector(workspace.Model.Handle.ClickDetector)
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Success!",
                        Content = "Got Null glove!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 5
                    })
                end
            end
            
        else
            -- Not in either required place, teleport to Null Zone
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Teleporting...",
                Content = "Going to Null Zone",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                Time = 3
            })
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(14422118326)
            end)
            
            if success then
                -- Queue script to get Null after teleport
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local nullScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(5458, -189, 1854)
                                wait(2)
                                if workspace:FindFirstChild("Model") and workspace.Model:FindFirstChild("Handle") and workspace.Model.Handle:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(workspace.Model.Handle.ClickDetector)
                                end
                            end
                        ]]
                        
                        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                            syn.queue_on_teleport(nullScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(nullScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

end

    Callback = function()
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
            -- Check if player has Pan glove equipped
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Pan" then
                -- Player has Pan equipped, teleport to position
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(18662, 2993, -298)
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Teleported!",
                        Content = "Pan user teleported to Tinkerer position",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 5
                    })
                end
            else
                -- Player doesn't have Pan equipped
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Pan glove first!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
            
        elseif currentPlaceId == 14422118326 then
            -- Already in Null Zone, get Tinkerer glove
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(4833.31, -214, 800.529)
                wait(2)
                for _, child in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if child:FindFirstChild("Handle") and child.Handle:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(child.Handle.ClickDetector)
                        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                            Name = "Success!",
                            Content = "Got Tinkerer glove!",
                            Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                            Time = 5
                        })
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
        else
            -- Not in either required place, teleport to Null Zone
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Teleporting...",
                Content = "Going to Null Zone",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                Time = 3
            })
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(14422118326)
            end)
            
            if success then
                -- Queue script to get Tinkerer after teleport
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local tinkererScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(4833.31, -214, 800.529)
                                wait(2)
                                for _, child in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                    if child:FindFirstChild("Handle") and child.Handle:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                                        fireclickdetector(child.Handle.ClickDetector)
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        ]]
                        
                        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                            syn.queue_on_teleport(tinkererScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(tinkererScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Necromancer",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

    local CandyCornCollector = "Teleport" -- Default fallback
local AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
local AutoServerhopCandyCorns = false

Tab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Choose Option To Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Default = "Teleport",
    Options = {"Teleport", "Bring"},
    Callback = function(Value)
        CandyCornCollector = Value
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoCollectCandyCorns = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if player already has the badge
            if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Already Have Badge",
                    Content = "You already have Necromancer glove badge! The farm will not work.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7734059095",
                    Time = 5
                })
                AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                return
            end
            
            if CandyCornCollector == "Teleport" then
                -- Auto Teleport to Candy Corns (BaseParts)
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        -- Check for badge again in case they got it during farming
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                                Name = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Image = "rbxassetid://7734059095",
                                Time = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            break
                        end
                        
                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local foundCandyCorn = false
                            
                            -- Search for BaseParts in CandyCorns folder
                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end
                                
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    foundCandyCorn = true
                                    -- Teleport to the BasePart
                                    character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(part.Position + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0))
                                    task.wait(0.2) -- Small delay between teleports
                                    break -- Focus on one at a time
                                end
                            end
                            
                            if not foundCandyCorn then
                                task.wait(0.5) -- Wait if no candy corns found
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
            elseif CandyCornCollector == "Bring" then
                -- Auto Bring Candy Corns (BaseParts) to player - directly to touch
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        -- Check for badge again in case they got it during farming
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                                Name = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Image = "rbxassetid://7734059095",
                                Time = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            break
                        end
                        
                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local humanoidRootPart = character.HumanoidRootPart
                            
                            -- Bring all BaseParts in CandyCorns folder directly to player
                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end
                                
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    -- Move the BasePart directly to player's position (touching)
                                    part.CFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Alchemist",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Global flag to control loop
_G.PlagueSlapRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.PlagueSlapRunning = state

        -- Teleport to random player (not self)
        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            else
                warn("Not enough players to teleport.")
            end
        end

        -- Fire PlagueHit on all players
        local function firePlagueHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("PlagueHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Main loop
        local function runAutoPlagueSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Plague") then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Plague glove.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                _G.PlagueSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.PlagueSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5) -- cooldown between hits
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                firePlagueHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoPlagueSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.PlagueSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Plague" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Arm"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Left Arm" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.PlagueHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Plague",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Druid",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport to Gardens And Ghouls Place (NOT AUTO GET GLOVE)",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local rep = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

        if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Alchemist" then
            rep.GeneralAbility:FireServer()

            local function mixItem(itemName, times)
                times = times or 1
                rep.Firework:InvokeServer()
                rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("AddItem", itemName)
                rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("EquipItem", itemName)
                for _ = 1, times do
                    rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("MixItem", itemName)
                end
            end

            -- Items to mix
            mixItem("Wild Vine", 3)
            mixItem("Blood Rose", 1)
            mixItem("Dark Root", 1)
            mixItem("Elder Wood", 1)
            mixItem("Jade Stone", 1)

            -- Final potion brew
            rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("BrewPotion")
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Alchemist Glove",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Jester",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Random Player",
    Callback = function()
        local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
        local localPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
        
        -- Remove local player from the list
        local otherPlayers = {}
        for _, player in pairs(players) do
            if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                table.insert(otherPlayers, player)
            end
        end
        
        if #otherPlayers > 0 then
            -- Select a random player
            local randomPlayer = otherPlayers[math.random(1, #otherPlayers)]
            
            if randomPlayer.Character and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local targetPosition = randomPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                localPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPosition)
                print("Teleported to random player: " .. randomPlayer.Name)
            else
                print("Selected player doesn't have valid character")
            end
        else
            print("No other players found to teleport to")
        end
    end
})

end
