do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Santa",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Jerry Boss Fight Place + Auto Get Santa",
    Callback = function()
local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
    -- First place (6403373529) - Snowpeeps and Teleport only
    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
    
    -- Click all Snowpeeps first (using correct path: workspace.Arena.XmasSnowPeeps)
    wait(0.2)
    local arena = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
    if arena then
        local xmasSnowPeeps = arena:FindFirstChild("XmasSnowPeeps")
        if xmasSnowPeeps then
            for _, peep in ipairs(xmasSnowPeeps:GetChildren()) do
                if peep:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                    fireclickdetector(peep.ClickDetector)
                    wait(0.1) -- Small delay between clicks
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- Teleport to position
    wait(0.2)
    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
        player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(2, -5, 353)
    end
    
elseif currentPlaceId == 95706409702231 then
    -- Second place (95706409702231) - Teleport and Anti-AFK
    -- This will auto-execute when arriving at the second place
    local function executeSecondPlaceScript()
        task.wait(20) -- Wait 20 seconds after arriving
        
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            -- Teleport to position
            player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-6, 21, -542)
            
            -- Enable Anti AFK
            _G.AntiAfk = true
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                if _G.AntiAfk then
                    VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                    VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                end
            end)
            
            print("Auto-executed: Teleported to position and enabled Anti-AFK")
        end
    end
    
    -- Auto-execute the function
    executeSecondPlaceScript()
end

-- Auto-execution for when teleporting from first place to second place
-- This sets up the script to run automatically after teleport
game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
        local targetPlaceId = 95706409702231 -- Second place ID
        local teleportScript = [[
            -- Wait for game to load
            wait(5)
            
            -- Check if we're in the target place
            if game.PlaceId == ]] .. targetPlaceId .. [[ then
                -- Wait 20 seconds, then execute
                task.wait(20)
                
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    -- Teleport to position
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-6, 21, -542)
                    
                    -- Enable Anti AFK
                    _G.AntiAfk = true
                    local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
                    
                    game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                        if _G.AntiAfk then
                            VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                            VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        ]]
        
        -- Queue the script to run after teleport
        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
            syn.queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
        elseif queue_on_teleport then
            queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
        end
    end
end)
end
})

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Blasphemy",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Bring Bus",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value) 
        Giftfarm = Value
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while Giftfarm do
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if not player then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                -- Find BusModel
                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "BusModel" then
                        pcall(function()
                            -- Method 1: Teleport the bus to the player (brings bus to you)
                            local busPrimaryPart = v:FindFirstChild("PrimaryPart") or v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or v:FindFirstChild("RootPart")
                            
                            if busPrimaryPart then
                                -- Move bus to player's position
                                busPrimaryPart.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                            else
                                -- If no primary part, move the whole model
                                local modelParts = {}
                                for _, part in pairs(v:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                        table.insert(modelParts, part)
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                -- Move each part to player
                                for _, part in pairs(modelParts) do
                                    part.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                            
                            -- Alternative: Move player to bus (if you want player to go to bus)
                            -- hrp.CFrame = v:GetPivot() + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                        end)
                    end
                end
                
                task.wait(0.05) -- Faster than original for better collection
            end
        end)
    end
})

end

    Name = "Teleport To Null Zone Place + Collect Rob Plushie",
    Callback = function()
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
            -- Check if player has Pan glove equipped
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Pan" then
                -- Player has Pan equipped, teleport to position
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(18662, 2993, -298)
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Teleported!",
                        Content = "Pan user teleported to Rob Plushie position",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 5
                    })
                end
            else
                -- Player doesn't have Pan equipped
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Pan glove first!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
            
        elseif currentPlaceId == 14422118326 then
            -- Already in Null Zone, get Rob Plushie
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(5259, -139, 861)
                wait(2)
                if workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectBobPlushie") and workspace._ugcQuestObjectBobPlushie:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                    fireclickdetector(workspace._ugcQuestObjectBobPlushie.ClickDetector)
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Success!",
                        Content = "Got Rob Plushie!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 5
                    })
                else
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Error",
                        Content = "Rob Plushie not found!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 5
                    })
                end
            end
            
        else
            -- Not in either required place, teleport to Null Zone
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Teleporting...",
                Content = "Going to Null Zone for Rob Plushie",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                Time = 3
            })
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(14422118326)
            end)
            
            if success then
                -- Queue script to get Rob Plushie after teleport
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local robScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(5259, -139, 861)
                                wait(2)
                                if workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectBobPlushie") and workspace._ugcQuestObjectBobPlushie:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(workspace._ugcQuestObjectBobPlushie.ClickDetector)
                                end
                            end
                        ]]
                        
                        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                            syn.queue_on_teleport(robScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(robScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To ? Place + Collect Alchemist Hood",
    Callback = function()

        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then

            })
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(11828384869)
            end)
            
            if success then
                -- Queue script to get Alchemist Hood after teleport
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local hoodScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local hrp = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local target = workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectEludeHat")
                            if target and target:FindFirstChild("Handle") and hrp then

                                    hrp.Anchored = false

                            syn.queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)

                            queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
            
        elseif currentPlaceId == 11828384869 then
            -- Already in ? place, get Alchemist Hood
            local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local hrp = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local target = workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectEludeHat")
            if target and target:FindFirstChild("Handle") and hrp then
                if hrp.Anchored then 
                    hrp.Anchored = false
                    task.wait(0.5) 
                end
                hrp.CFrame = target.Handle.CFrame
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Success!",
                    Content = "Got Alchemist Hood!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Alchemist Hood not found!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
            
        else
            -- Not in either required place, teleport to ? place
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Teleporting...",
                Content = "Going to ? place for Alchemist Hood",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                Time = 3
            })
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(11828384869)
            end)
            
            if success then
                -- Queue script to get Alchemist Hood after teleport
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local hoodScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local hrp = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local target = workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectEludeHat")
                            if target and target:FindFirstChild("Handle") and hrp then
                                if hrp.Anchored then 
                                    hrp.Anchored = false
                                    task.wait(0.5) 
                                end
                                hrp.CFrame = target.Handle.CFrame
                            end
                        ]]
                        
                        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                            syn.queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 5
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Admin",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To The Staff Application Place (NOT AUTO GET GLOVE)",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 16034567693
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        -- Function to execute Admin script
        local function executeAdminScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                game.Loaded:Wait()
            end

            if getgenv().AutoGetAdminExecuted == true then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetAdminExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                -- Second place: Staff Application
                task.wait(10)
                
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(502, 76, 59)
                end
                
                task.wait(10)
                
                -- Anti-afk
                if getconnections then
                    for i,v in next, getconnections(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Idled) do
                        v:Disable() 
                    end
                else
                    while task.wait(10) do
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Jump = true
                        end
                    end
                end
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId then
                -- First place: Slap Battles
                if game.ReplicatedStorage.Assets:FindFirstChild("Retro") then
                    game.ReplicatedStorage.Assets.Retro.Parent = workspace
                end
                
                repeat task.wait(10) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Retro")
                
                task.wait(10)
                
                for i,v in pairs(workspace.Retro.Map.RetroObbyMap:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "Model" and v:FindFirstChild("StaffApp") and v.StaffApp:FindFirstChild("Button") and v.StaffApp.Button:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v.StaffApp.Button.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,50,0)
                            task.wait(10)
                            fireclickdetector(v.StaffApp.Button.ClickDetector)
                        end
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    -- Save the Admin script to re-execute after teleport
                    local adminScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then
                            game.Loaded:Wait()
                        end
                        task.wait(10)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 16034567693
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            -- Auto-execute in second place
                            task.wait(10)
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(502, 76, 59)
                            end
                            task.wait(10)
                            if getconnections then
                                for i,v in next, getconnections(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Idled) do
                                    v:Disable() 
                                end
                            else
                                while task.wait(10) do
                                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Jump = true
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(adminScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(adminScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeAdminScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            
            if not success then
                if connection then
                    connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

end

        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Joust" then
                    found = true
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Joust glove.",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Joust glove",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Joust Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Joust" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Joust Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

    Name = "Auto Parry (Ability)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility2s = Value
        
        if Value then
            print("Auto General Ability started - firing every 2 seconds")
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility2s and task.wait(2) do
                    local success, error = pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
                    end)
                    
                    if success then
                        print("Fired GeneralAbility remote")
                    else
                        warn("Failed to fire GeneralAbility:", error)
                    end
                end
            end)
        else

        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Touch Labyrinth Doors",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(Value)
		_G.AutoLabyrinth = Value
		
		task.spawn(function()
			while _G.AutoLabyrinth do
				local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
				if not player then 
					task.wait(0.1) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local char = player.Character
				if not char or not char.Parent then 
					-- Wait for character to load
					char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
					task.wait(0.5)
					continue 
				end
				
				local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if not hrp then 
					task.wait(0.01) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local doorsFound = 0
				
				for _, labyrinth in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
					if string.find(labyrinth.Name, "Labyrinth") and labyrinth:FindFirstChild("Doors") then
						for _, door in ipairs(labyrinth.Doors:GetChildren()) do
							local hitbox = door:FindFirstChild("Hitbox")
							if hitbox and hitbox:IsA("BasePart") then
								doorsFound = doorsFound + 1
								pcall(function()
									-- Method 1: Teleport player directly into the hitbox multiple times
									for i = 1, 8 do
										hrp.CFrame = hitbox.CFrame
										task.wait(0.02)
									end
									
									-- Move slightly forward into the door
									hrp.CFrame = hitbox.CFrame + hitbox.CFrame.LookVector * 2
									task.wait(0.1)
									
									-- Shake/teleport inside hitbox to ensure trigger
									for i = 1, 5 do
										hrp.CFrame = hitbox.CFrame
										task.wait(0.01)
									end
									
									task.wait(0.3)
								end)
							end
						end
					end
				end
				
				-- Adjust wait time based on whether doors were found
				if doorsFound == 0 then
					task.wait(0.5) -- No doors, wait longer
				else
					task.wait(0.2) -- Doors found, fast loop
				end
			end
		end)
	end
})

end

                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3

        end

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Pocket Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Pocket" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Pocket Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Get Knockoff Glove",
    Callback = function()

    local buttonsToPress = {4, 5, 5, 3, 2, 9, 3}
    local foundRoom = false

    for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
        local character = player.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            local roomName = player.Name .. "'s Room"
            local room = workspace.RoomsFolder:FindFirstChild(roomName)

            if room and room:FindFirstChild("PocketKeypad") then
                local keypad = room.PocketKeypad
                local buttons = keypad:FindFirstChild("Buttons")

                if buttons then
                    foundRoom = true

                    -- Press each number in the sequence
                    for _, num in ipairs(buttonsToPress) do
                        local button = buttons:FindFirstChild(tostring(num))
                        if button then
                            local cd = button:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                            if cd then
                                fireclickdetector(cd)
                                wait(0.15)
                            end
                        end
                    end

                    -- Press Enter
                    local enterButton = buttons:FindFirstChild("Enter")
                    if enterButton then
                        local cd = enterButton:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                        if cd then
                            fireclickdetector(cd)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    if not foundRoom then
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "No one is in the arena!",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
    end
end
})

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Frostbite",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Ice Trials Place + Get Ice Essence",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 17290438723
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        -- Function to execute the item script
        local function executeItemScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                game.Loaded:Wait()
            end

            -- Credits, message is not squished up cuz it looks bad
            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Credits to Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Made by @nexer1234 ( youtube & discord )",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Thanks!"
            })

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Please re-execute script after teleporting",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Oh..."
            })

            if game.PlaceId == 17290438723 then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-555, 180, 55)
                wait(1)
                for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.ClassName == "ProximityPrompt" then
                        if v.HoldDuration ~= 0 then
                            v.HoldDuration = 0
                        end
                        if v.RequiresLineOfSight ~= false then
                            v.RequiresLineOfSight = false
                        end
                        if v.MaxActivationDistance ~= 9e9 then
                            v.MaxActivationDistance = 9e9
                        end
                        v.Enabled = true
                        fireproximityprompt(v)
                    end
                end
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(17290438723) end
            else
                game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                    Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                    Text = "Wrong game buddy",
                    Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                    Duration = 36000,
                    Button1 = "Oh..."
                })
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    -- Save the script to re-execute after teleport
                    local itemScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then
                            game.Loaded:Wait()
                        end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == 17290438723 then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-555, 180, 55)
                            wait(1)
                            for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.ClassName == "ProximityPrompt" then
                                    if v.HoldDuration ~= 0 then
                                        v.HoldDuration = 0
                                    end
                                    if v.RequiresLineOfSight ~= false then
                                        v.RequiresLineOfSight = false
                                    end
                                    if v.MaxActivationDistance ~= 9e9 then
                                        v.MaxActivationDistance = 9e9
                                    end
                                    v.Enabled = true
                                    fireproximityprompt(v)
                                end
                            end
                        elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                            while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(17290438723) end
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    -- Use syn.queue_on_teleport or queue_on_teleport depending on executor
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            -- We're already in the target place, execute item script
            print("Already in target place - executing item script")
            executeItemScript()
        else
            -- We're not in the target place, teleport to the game
            print("Teleporting to target game...")
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            
            if not success then
                print("Teleport failed:", errorMsg)
                if connection then
                    connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

end

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Spoonful",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- ===== VARIABLES =====
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

-- Variables
local isAutoClicking = false
local pointsWaiting = false
local pointsStarted = false
local pointsStopped = false
local pointsFinished = false
local selfDestructClicks = 0
local requiredSelfDestructClicks = 100
local requiredPoints = 5000
local isAntiAfkEnabled = false
local ownSlapBattlesSweepBadge = false
local autoClickLoop = nil

-- Badge display variables
local badgeStatusText = "Loading..."

-- SLAP BATTLES SWEEP Badge ID
local SLAP_BATTLES_SWEEP_BADGE_ID = 2236076719770808

-- Get player's tycoon model name (supports both encodings)
local function getTycoonModelNames()
    local username = player.Name
    -- Return both possibilities - will check both when searching
    return {"\195\133Tycoon" .. username, "\195\129Tycoon" .. username}
end

-- Function to find tycoon (checks both name variations)
local function findTycoon()
    local names = getTycoonModelNames()
    for _, name in ipairs(names) do
        local tycoon = workspace:FindFirstChild(name)
        if tycoon then
            return tycoon, name
        end
    end
    return nil, nil
end

-- Function to get current points from Counter
local function getCurrentPoints()
    local tycoon = findTycoon()
    if tycoon then
        local counter = tycoon:FindFirstChild("Counter")
        if counter then
            local part = counter:FindFirstChild("Part")
            if part then
                local surfaceGui = part:FindFirstChild("SurfaceGui")
                if surfaceGui then
                    local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                    if textLabel and textLabel:IsA("TextLabel") then
                        local text = textLabel.Text
                        local number = tonumber(text:match("%d+")) or 0
                        return number
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return 0
end

-- Function to get self destruct clicks from SDCounter
local function getSelfDestructClicks()
    local tycoon = findTycoon()
    if tycoon then
        local sdCounter = tycoon:FindFirstChild("SDCounter")
        if sdCounter then
            local counter = sdCounter:FindFirstChild("Counter")
            if counter then
                local part = counter:FindFirstChild("Part")
                if part then
                    local surfaceGui = part:FindFirstChild("SurfaceGui")
                    if surfaceGui then
                        local textLabel = surfaceGui:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                        if textLabel and textLabel:IsA("TextLabel") then
                            local text = textLabel.Text
                            local number = tonumber(text:match("%d+")) or 0
                            return number
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return nil
end

-- Function to check if SLAP BATTLES SWEEP badge is owned
local function checkSlapBattlesSweepBadge()
    local userId = player.UserId
    local url = "https://badges.roblox.com/v1/users/" .. userId .. "/badges?limit=100&sortOrder=Asc"
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet(url)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(response)
        if data and data.data then
            for _, badge in ipairs(data.data) do
                if badge.id == SLAP_BATTLES_SWEEP_BADGE_ID then
                    ownSlapBattlesSweepBadge = true
                    return true
                end
            end
        end
    end
    ownSlapBattlesSweepBadge = false
    return false
end

-- Function to update badge status text
local function updateBadgeStatusText()
    local badgeStatus = ownSlapBattlesSweepBadge and "✅ Yes" or "❌ No"
    badgeStatusText = string.format([[
Owns SLAP BATTLES SWEEP Badge: %s
SLAP BATTLES SWEEP Badge Awards Glove: Spoonful Glove
]],
    badgeStatus
)
    return badgeStatusText
end

-- Function to update points status display
local function updatePointsDisplay()
    local currentPoints = getCurrentPoints()
    local autoClickStatus = isAutoClicking and "Yes" or "No"
    local antiAfkStatus = isAntiAfkEnabled and "Yes" or "No"
    local selfDestructDisplay = "Not Found"
    
    local sdValue = getSelfDestructClicks()
    if sdValue ~= nil then
        selfDestructDisplay = sdValue .. "/" .. requiredSelfDestructClicks
    end
    
    -- Points Show status logic
    local waitingStatus = "Waiting to start..."
    local startedStatus = "Not Started"
    local stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
    local finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    
    if pointsFinished then
        waitingStatus = "Finished!"
        startedStatus = requiredPoints .. "/" .. requiredPoints
        stoppedStatus = "N/A"
        finishedStatus = requiredPoints .. "/" .. requiredPoints
    elseif pointsStopped then
        waitingStatus = "Stopped"
        startedStatus = currentPoints .. "/" .. requiredPoints
        stoppedStatus = currentPoints .. "/" .. requiredPoints
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    elseif pointsStarted then
        waitingStatus = "Running..."
        startedStatus = currentPoints .. "/" .. requiredPoints
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    elseif not isAutoClicking then
        waitingStatus = "Ready to start"
        startedStatus = "Not Started"
        stoppedStatus = "Not Stopped"
        finishedStatus = "Not Finished"
    end
    
    local statusText = string.format([[
Points Show Waiting: %s
Points Show Started: %s
Points Show Stopped: %s
Points Show Finished: %s
AutoClick: %s
Self Destruct Button Clicked Times: %s
Anti AFK: %s
]],
    waitingStatus,
    startedStatus,
    stoppedStatus,
    finishedStatus,
    autoClickStatus,
    selfDestructDisplay,
    antiAfkStatus
    )
    
    return statusText
end

-- Create the TWO paragraphs
local TycoonStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Tycoon Status:", "Loading...")
local BadgeStatusParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph("Badge Status:", "Loading badge info...")

-- ===== LOOP: TYCOON STATUS UPDATE =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        local statusText = updatePointsDisplay()
        pcall(function()
            TycoonStatusParagraph:Set(statusText)
        end)
        task.wait(0.5)
    end
end)

-- ===== LOOP: BADGE STATUS UPDATE (5 SECONDS) =====
task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        checkSlapBattlesSweepBadge()
        local badgeText = updateBadgeStatusText()
        pcall(function()
            BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(badgeText)
        end)
        task.wait(5)
    end
end)

-- ===== AUTO CLICK TYCOON TOGGLE =====
_G.AutoTycoon = false

AutoClickTycoon = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Click Tycoon",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoTycoon = Value
        isAutoClicking = Value
        
        if Value then
            pointsStarted = true
            pointsStopped = false
            pointsFinished = false
            pointsWaiting = false
            
            if autoClickLoop then
                task.cancel(autoClickLoop)
                autoClickLoop = nil
            end
            
            autoClickLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while _G.AutoTycoon do
                    -- Check if points reached required amount
                    local currentPoints = getCurrentPoints()
                    if currentPoints >= requiredPoints then
                        pointsFinished = true
                        pointsStarted = false
                        _G.AutoTycoon = false
                        AutoClickTycoon:Set(false)
                        
                        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                            Name = "Tycoon",
                            Content = "Goal reached! " .. currentPoints .. "/" .. requiredPoints .. " points!",
                            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                            Time = 5
                        })
                        break
                    end
                    
                    pcall(function()
                        local tycoon = findTycoon()
                        if tycoon then
                            local clickPart = tycoon:FindFirstChild("Click")
                            if clickPart and clickPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                                local detector = clickPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                                if detector then
                                    fireclickdetector(detector)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait()
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Click Tycoon",
                Content = "Started! Need " .. requiredPoints .. " points",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            if autoClickLoop then
                task.cancel(autoClickLoop)
                autoClickLoop = nil
            end
            pointsStopped = true
            pointsStarted = false
            
            local currentPoints = getCurrentPoints()

        end
    end
})

-- ===== ANTI AFK TOGGLE =====
AntiAfk = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        isAntiAfkEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end    
})

-- Initial updates
checkSlapBattlesSweepBadge()
BadgeStatusParagraph:Set(updateBadgeStatusText())
TycoonStatusParagraph:Set(updatePointsDisplay())

    Tab:AddButton({

    end

-- Function to fire the ClickDetector for a player
local function fireClickForPlayer(player)
    -- Fire the ClickDetector when a player touches it
    clickDetector:Fire(player)
end

-- Connect to the player joining event
game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
    -- You can also set up a way to detect when a player interacts with the ClickDetector
    -- You can use Touched or other events to trigger the FireClickDetector function.

    -- Optionally, you can fire the ClickDetector when the player touches the part
    part.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        -- Check if the part hit is a player's character
        local character = hit.Parent
        if character:IsA("Model") and character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            fireClickForPlayer(player)
        end
    end)
end)
wait()
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Tycoon",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Siphon",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

local G_ = {}
G_.SiphonAuto = false

Tab:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Bring Siphon Orb",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(Value)
		G_.SiphonAuto = Value
		
		task.spawn(function()
			while G_.SiphonAuto do
				local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
				if not player then 
					task.wait(0.1) 
					continue 
				end
				
				-- Check slaps requirement
				if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Slaps and player.leaderstats.Slaps.Value < 0 then
					G_.SiphonAuto = false
					OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "0+ Slaps Required", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
					break
				end
				
				local character = player.Character
				if not character or not character.Parent then 
					task.wait(0.01) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local head = character:FindFirstChild("Head")
				if not head then 
					task.wait(0.01) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local orbsFound = 0
				
				-- Find all Siphon Orbs
				for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
					if v.Name == "SiphonOrb" then
						orbsFound = orbsFound + 1
						pcall(function()
							-- Teleport Siphon Orb directly to player's head
							if v:IsA("BasePart") then
								-- Orb is a single part
								v.CFrame = head.CFrame
							elseif v:IsA("Model") then
								-- Orb is a model
								local orbPart = v:FindFirstChild("Handle") or v:FindFirstChild("OrbPart") or v:FindFirstChild("PrimaryPart")
								
								if orbPart then
									orbPart.CFrame = head.CFrame
								else
									-- Move all parts to player's head
									for _, part in pairs(v:GetDescendants()) do
										if part:IsA("BasePart") then
											part.CFrame = head.CFrame
										end
									end
								end
							end
						end)
					end
				end
				
				-- Adjust wait time based on whether orbs were found
				if orbsFound == 0 then
					task.wait(0.3) -- No orbs, wait a bit
				else
					task.wait(0.05) -- Orbs found, fast loop
				end
			end
		end)
	end
})

end

                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Thor glove",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Thor Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Thor" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Thor Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Spawn Sentry",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Engineer" then
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Sentry:FireServer()
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({ Name = "Error", Content = "Equip Engineer Glove", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3 })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Turret",
    Callback = function()
            local turret = game.workspace:FindFirstChild("Turret")
            if turret and turret:FindFirstChild("HingePart") and turret.HingePart:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = turret.HingePart.Glove.CFrame
        end
    end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Hunter",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- First Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Guide Place + Get Hunter Glove",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 18550498098
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        -- Function to execute the item script
        local function executeItemScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                game.Loaded:Wait()
            end

            function Checkamogus()
                DontGetAvatar = true
                repeat task.wait() until DontGetAvatar ~= nil

                if DontGetAvatar == true then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -65, 824)
                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["the cube of life"].Part.CFrame
                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["Big Heart"].CFrame
                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                end
            end

            -- Credits, message is not squished up cuz it looks bad
            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Credits to Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Made by @nexer1234 ( youtube & discord )",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Thanks!"
            })

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Please re-execute script after teleporting",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Oh..."
            })

            if game.PlaceId == 18550498098 then
                Checkamogus()
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                end
                wait(5)
                for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.Name == "ShackLever" and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                    end
                end
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                end
                repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace.Map.Components:FindFirstChild("GuideNPC")
                task.wait(.8)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(599, 250, -322)
                task.wait(.8)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true

                while task.wait(.1) do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Lantern") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Lantern.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    end
                    --game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.Data.AnswerInCutscene:FireServer("Spare")

                    for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == "PusherWall" then
                            v.CanCollide = false
                        end

                        if v.Name == "DungeonGolem" and v:FindFirstChild("Cube.001") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v["Cube.001"])
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "golem" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.Hitbox)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "ReplicaNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "GuideNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "TrackGloveMissile" then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                Instance.new("Message",game.CoreGui).Text = "You're being teleported, please wait, it may take up to a minute..."

                for i,v in pairs(workspace.BountyHunterRoom:GetChildren()) do
                    if v and v:IsA('Model') and v:FindFirstChild('Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005') then
                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters" then
                            if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                            end
                            while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                        else
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters"
                            if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                            end
                            while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                    Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                    Text = "Wrong game buddy",
                    Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                    Duration = 36000,
                    Button1 = "Oh..."
                })
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    -- Save the script to re-execute after teleport
                    local itemScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then
                            game.Loaded:Wait()
                        end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        function Checkamogus()
                            DontGetAvatar = true
                            repeat task.wait() until DontGetAvatar ~= nil

                            if DontGetAvatar == true then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -65, 824)
                                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                                end
                                wait(5)
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["the cube of life"].Part.CFrame
                                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                                end
                                wait(5)
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["Big Heart"].CFrame
                                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                                end
                                wait(5)
                            end
                        end

                        if game.PlaceId == 18550498098 then
                            Checkamogus()
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                game.Loaded:Wait()
                            end
                            wait(5)
                            for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.Name == "ShackLever" and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                                end
                            end
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                game.Loaded:Wait()
                            end
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace.Map.Components:FindFirstChild("GuideNPC")
                            task.wait(.8)
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(599, 250, -322)
                            task.wait(.8)
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true

                            while task.wait(.1) do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Lantern") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Lantern.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                end
                                --game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.Data.AnswerInCutscene:FireServer("Spare")

                                for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v.Name == "PusherWall" then
                                        v.CanCollide = false
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "DungeonGolem" and v:FindFirstChild("Cube.001") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v["Cube.001"])
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "golem" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.Hitbox)
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "ReplicaNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "GuideNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "TrackGloveMissile" then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                            Instance.new("Message",game.CoreGui).Text = "You're being teleported, please wait, it may take up to a minute..."

                            for i,v in pairs(workspace.BountyHunterRoom:GetChildren()) do
                                if v and v:IsA('Model') and v:FindFirstChild('Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005') then
                                    if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters" then
                                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                                        end
                                        while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                                    else
                                        repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters"
                                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                                        end
                                        while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            -- We're already in the target place, execute item script
            print("Already in target place - executing item script")
            executeItemScript()
        else
            -- We're not in the target place, teleport to the game
            print("Teleporting to target game...")
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            
            if not success then
                print("Teleport failed:", errorMsg)
                if connection then
                    connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

                            end
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace.Map.Components:FindFirstChild("GuideNPC")
                            task.wait(.8)
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(599, 250, -322)
                            task.wait(.8)
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true

                            while task.wait(.1) do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Lantern") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Lantern.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                end
                                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.Data.AnswerInCutscene:FireServer("Spare")

                                for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v.Name == "PusherWall" then
                                        v.CanCollide = false
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "DungeonGolem" and v:FindFirstChild("Cube.001") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v["Cube.001"])
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "golem" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.Hitbox)
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "ReplicaNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "GuideNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "TrackGloveMissile" then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                            Instance.new("Message",game.CoreGui).Text = "You're being teleported, please wait, it may take up to a minute..."

                            for i,v in pairs(workspace.BountyHunterRoom:GetChildren()) do
                                if v and v:IsA('Model') and v:FindFirstChild('Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005') then
                                    if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters" then
                                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                                        end
                                        while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                                    else
                                        repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters"
                                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                                        end
                                        while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            -- We're already in the target place, execute item script
            print("Already in target place - executing item script")
            executeItemScript()
        else
            -- We're not in the target place, teleport to the game
            print("Teleporting to target game...")
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            
            if not success then
                print("Teleport failed:", errorMsg)
                if connection then
                    connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end
})
