do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Fan",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})
    
-- Fan Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To barzil Place + Get Fan",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 7234087065
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeFanScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Credits to Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Made by @nexer1234 ( youtube & discord )",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Thanks!"
            })

            if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.QuestStuff.Key.CFrame
                task.wait(1.5)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.SuitUpClown:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyQuest:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyAcquired:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.GOHOME:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyBadgeReward:FireServer()
                task.wait(1.5)
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(7234087065) end
            else
                game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                    Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                    Text = "Wrong game buddy",
                    Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                    Duration = 36000,
                    Button1 = "Oh..."
                })
            end
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeFanScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local fanScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.QuestStuff.Key.CFrame
                            task.wait(1.5)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.SuitUpClown:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyQuest:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyAcquired:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.GOHOME:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyBadgeReward:FireServer()
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then syn.queue_on_teleport(fanScript) else queue_on_teleport(fanScript) end
                end
            end)
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function() TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId) end)
            if not success and connection then connection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end
})

end

Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Boxer",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",

-- Boxer Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To barzil Place + Get Boxer",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 7234087065
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeBoxerScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(4231.26123046875, 3510.86376953125, 270.4519958496094)
                repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace:FindFirstChild("BoxingGloves")
                task.wait(1)
                fireclickdetector(workspace.BoxingGloves.ClickDetector)
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(7234087065) end
            end
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeBoxerScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local boxerScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(4231.26123046875, 3510.86376953125, 270.4519958496094)
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace:FindFirstChild("BoxingGloves")
                            task.wait(1)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace.BoxingGloves.ClickDetector)
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then syn.queue_on_teleport(boxerScript) else queue_on_teleport(boxerScript) end
                end
            end)
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function() TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId) end)
            if not success and connection then connection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end
})

do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "MATERIALIZE",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Bring MATERIALIZE Orb",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(Value)
		_G.Materializefarm = Value
		
		task.spawn(function()
			while _G.Materializefarm do
				local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
				if not player then 
					task.wait(0.1) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local character = player.Character
				if not character or not character.Parent then 
					task.wait(0.01) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local head = character:FindFirstChild("Head")
				if not head then 
					task.wait(0.01) 
					continue 
				end
				
				local orbsFound = 0
				
				-- Find all MATERIALIZE Orbs
				for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
					if v.Name == "MATERIALIZEOrb" then
						orbsFound = orbsFound + 1
						pcall(function()
							-- Teleport MATERIALIZE Orb directly to player's head
							if v:IsA("BasePart") then
								-- Orb is a single part
								v.CFrame = head.CFrame
							elseif v:IsA("Model") then
								-- Orb is a model
								local orbPart = v:FindFirstChild("Handle") or v:FindFirstChild("OrbPart") or v:FindFirstChild("PrimaryPart")
								
								if orbPart then
									orbPart.CFrame = head.CFrame
								else
									-- Move all parts to player's head
									for _, part in pairs(v:GetDescendants()) do
										if part:IsA("BasePart") then
											part.CFrame = head.CFrame
										end
									end
								end
							end
						end)
					end
				end
				
				-- Adjust wait time based on whether orbs were found
				if orbsFound == 0 then
					task.wait(0.5) -- No orbs, wait longer
				else
					task.wait(0.05) -- Orbs found, fast loop
				end
			end
		end)
	end    
})

end
do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Bind",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Bind Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Binded Maze Place + Get Bind",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 74169485398268
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeBindScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            if game.PlaceId == 74169485398268 then
                local time = tick()
                while tick() - time < 10 do task.wait() fireclickdetector(workspace.Orb:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")) end
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(6403373529) end
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(74169485398268) end
            end
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeBindScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local bindScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        if game.PlaceId == 74169485398268 then
                            local time = tick()
                            while tick() - time < 10 do task.wait() fireclickdetector(workspace.Orb:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")) end
                            while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(6403373529) end
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then syn.queue_on_teleport(bindScript) else queue_on_teleport(bindScript) end
                end
            end)
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function() TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId) end)
            if not success and connection then connection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end
})

end
do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Poltergeist",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Poltergeist Button with Auto-Execute
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Zombies Place + Get Poltergeist",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 103505724406848
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executePoltergeistScript()
            loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/MaaZiusz/sb/refs/heads/main/Poltergeist"))()
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executePoltergeistScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local poltergeistScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/MaaZiusz/sb/refs/heads/main/Poltergeist"))()
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then 
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(poltergeistScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(poltergeistScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            
            if not success then
                print("Teleport failed:", errorMsg)
                if connection then
                    connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

end
do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Clock",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Clock Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To FNAO Place (NOT AUTO GETS GLOVE)",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 7234087065
        local thirdPlaceId = 102908326578005
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeClockScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetClockExecuted then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetClockExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == thirdPlaceId then
                -- Third place: FNAO - Get Clock
                print("In third place - getting Clock")
                for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                end
                task.wait(2)
                for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                end
                task.wait(2)
                while task.wait() do 
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(26.34327507019043, 4.055271148681641, -1.8455318212509155) 
                    end
                end
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                -- Second place: Barzil - Teleport to wizard tower
                print("In second place - going to wizard tower")
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(249.473419, 157.87326, -458.792145, 0.707134247, -0, -0.707079291, 0, 1, -0, 0.707079291, 0, 0.707134247)
                end
                task.wait(3)
                while task.wait() do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        for i,v in pairs(workspace.Buildings:GetChildren()) do
                            if v.Name == "wizard twoer" and v:FindFirstChild("Cone") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v.Cone.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,15,0)
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                -- First place or other Slap Battles places - Teleport to second place
                print("In first place - teleporting to second place")
                while task.wait() do 
                    game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId) 
                end
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring for ALL places
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local clockScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetClockExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 7234087065
                        local thirdPlaceId = 102908326578005
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == thirdPlaceId then
                            -- Auto-execute in third place
                            print("Auto-executing in third place")
                            for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                            end
                            task.wait(2)
                            for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                            end
                            task.wait(2)
                            while task.wait() do 
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(26.34327507019043, 4.055271148681641, -1.8455318212509155) 
                                end
                            end
                            
                        elseif game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            -- Auto-execute in second place
                            print("Auto-executing in second place")
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(249.473419, 157.87326, -458.792145, 0.707134247, -0, -0.707079291, 0, 1, -0, 0.707079291, 0, 0.707134247)
                            end
                            task.wait(3)
                            while task.wait() do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    for i,v in pairs(workspace.Buildings:GetChildren()) do
                                        if v.Name == "wizard twoer" and v:FindFirstChild("Cone") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v.Cone.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,15,0)
                                            break
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then 
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(clockScript) 
                    else 
                        queue_on_teleport(clockScript) 
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId or currentPlaceId == thirdPlaceId then
            print("Already in target place - executing script")
            executeClockScript()
        else
            print("Not in target place - setting up teleport monitor")
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function() 
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId) 
            end)
            
            if not success then
                print("Teleport failed:", errorMsg)
                if connection then connection:Disconnect() end
            end
        end
    end
})

    Callback = function()

        local foundPlayer = nil

            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "ZZZZZZZ" then

                    break

            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "ZZZZZZZ Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Leg"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                [2] = false  -- The second argument, set to false as in your original script
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Left Leg" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end

end

        if xmasSnowPeeps then

                    wait(0.1) -- Small delay between clicks

            end
        end
    end

    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
        player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(2, -5, 353)

    -- Second place (95706409702231) - Teleport, Anti-AFK, and Boss manipulation
    -- This will auto-execute when arriving at the second place

        task.wait(20) -- Wait 20 seconds after arriving
        
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            -- Teleport to position
            player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-6, 21, -542)
            
            -- Enable Anti AFK
            _G.AntiAfk = true
            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
            
            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                if _G.AntiAfk then
                    VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                    VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                end
            end)
            
            -- Start boss health manipulation
            local bossManipulationThread = task.spawn(function()
                while task.wait(0.01) do
                    local boss = workspace:FindFirstChild("Boss")
                    if boss and boss:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                        boss.Humanoid.Health = 1
                        task.wait(0.02)
                        boss.Humanoid.Health = 0
                    else
                        -- Wait a bit if boss isn't found yet
                        task.wait(1)
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            -- Store the thread reference so it can be stopped if needed
            _G.BossManipulationThread = bossManipulationThread
            
            print("Auto-executed: Teleported to position, enabled Anti-AFK, and started boss manipulation")
        end
    end
    
    -- Auto-execute the function
    executeSecondPlaceScript()
end

    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
        local targetPlaceId = 95706409702231 -- Second place ID

            -- Wait for game to load
            wait(5)
            
            -- Check if we're in the target place

                    -- Teleport to position

                        if _G.AntiAfk then
                            VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                            VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                        end
                    end)
                    
                    -- Start boss health manipulation
                    local bossManipulationThread = task.spawn(function()
                        while task.wait(0.01) do
                            local boss = workspace:FindFirstChild("Boss")
                            if boss and boss:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                                boss.Humanoid.Health = 1
                                task.wait(0.02)
                                boss.Humanoid.Health = 0
                            else
                                -- Wait a bit if boss isn't found yet
                                task.wait(1)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    
                    -- Store the thread reference so it can be stopped if needed
                    _G.BossManipulationThread = bossManipulationThread
                end
            end
        ]]
        
        -- Queue the script to run after teleport
        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
            syn.queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
        elseif queue_on_teleport then
            queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
        end
    end
end)

do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Draw4",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

getgenv().AutoPingPongReal = false
local autoPingPongLoop = nil

local function CheckGlove()
    local leaderstats = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
    if leaderstats then
        local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
        if glove then
            return glove.Value
        end
    end
    return nil
end

local function startPingPongLoop()
    if autoPingPongLoop then return end
    
    autoPingPongLoop = task.spawn(function()
        while getgenv().AutoPingPongReal do
            if CheckGlove() == "Ping Pong" then
                local character = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character
                if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    for _, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name:find("_PingPongBall") and (character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v.Position).Magnitude <= 48 then
                            pcall(function()
                                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("PingPongEvent"):FireServer()
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end)
end

local function stopPingPongLoop()
    if autoPingPongLoop then
        task.cancel(autoPingPongLoop)
        autoPingPongLoop = nil
    end
end

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Ping Pong",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        getgenv().AutoPingPongReal = state
        if state then
            startPingPongLoop()
        else
            stopPingPongLoop()
        end
    end
})

end

    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Mouse",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false

-- Mouse Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Cheese Place + Get Mouse",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 97220865182663
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeMouseScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetMouseExecuted then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetMouseExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                -- Second place: Cheese Place - Kill rats and get Mouse
                if workspace.Game.Buildings.City:FindFirstChild("City") == nil then
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.PlaceBuilding:FireServer("City", Vector3.new(3.125, 43.4450798034668, -57.1875), 0)
                end

                while task.wait(.003) do
                    for i,v in pairs(workspace.Game.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == "Rat" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health ~= 0 then
                            v.Hitbox.Anchored = true
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.GloveHit:FireServer(v.Hitbox)
                            v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                        end
                    end
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.UnlockGloveWithOrbs:FireServer()
                end
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                -- First place: Slap Battles - Get el gato and click Cheese
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") == nil then
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value >= 11500 then
                        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["el gato"].ClickDetector)
                        repeat task.wait(.1) until game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "el gato"
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Lobby["Teleport1"].CFrame
                        repeat task.wait(.1) until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        task.wait(.1)
                        fireclickdetector(workspace.Cheese.ClickDetector)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local mouseScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetMouseExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 97220865182663
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            -- Auto-execute in second place
                            if workspace.Game.Buildings.City:FindFirstChild("City") == nil then
                                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.PlaceBuilding:FireServer("City", Vector3.new(3.125, 43.4450798034668, -57.1875), 0)
                            end
                            while task.wait(.003) do
                                for i,v in pairs(workspace.Game.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v.Name == "Rat" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health ~= 0 then
                                        v.Hitbox.Anchored = true
                                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.GloveHit:FireServer(v.Hitbox)
                                        v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                                    end
                                end
                                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.UnlockGloveWithOrbs:FireServer()
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then 
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(mouseScript) 
                    else 
                        queue_on_teleport(mouseScript) 
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeMouseScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function() 
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId) 
            end)
            
            if not success then
                if connection then connection:Disconnect() end
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Hexa Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To White Place + Get Hexa",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 98726100529621
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeHexaScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetHexaExecuted then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetHexaExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                -- Second place: White Place - Complete obby and get Hexa
                repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part I") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                task.wait(5)
                workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CanCollide = false
                workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CanTouch = true
                workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 2") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                task.wait(5)
                workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CanCollide = false
                workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CanTouch = true
                workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace["Part 2"]:FindFirstChild("Portal")
                workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CanCollide = false
                workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CanTouch = true
                workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 3") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                task.wait(5)
                fireclickdetector(workspace["Part 3"].TpToNext.HitBox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 4") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                task.wait(5)
                workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CanCollide = false
                workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CanTouch = true
                workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 5") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                task.wait(5)
                fireclickdetector(workspace["Part 5"].Glove.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Finale") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                task.wait(5)
                fireclickdetector(workspace.Finale.Reward.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                -- First place: Slap Battles - Check for Obby glove and teleport
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Obby" then
                    -- Player has Obby glove equipped, teleport to White Place
                    game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)
                else
                    -- Player doesn't have Obby glove equipped
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Obby glove first!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 5
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local hexaScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetHexaExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 98726100529621
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            -- Auto-execute in second place
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part I") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 2") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace["Part 2"]:FindFirstChild("Portal")
                            workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 3") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace["Part 3"].TpToNext.HitBox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 4") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 5") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace["Part 5"].Glove.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Finale") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace.Finale.Reward.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then 
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(hexaScript) 
                    else 
                        queue_on_teleport(hexaScript) 
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeHexaScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function() 
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId) 
            end)
            
            if not success then
                if connection then connection:Disconnect() end
            end
        end
    end
})

do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Swordfighter",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Swordfighter Button
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Sword Fight Place + Get Swordfighter",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 117232463555132
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeSwordfighterScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            if getgenv().AutoGetSwordfighterExecuted == true then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetSwordfighterExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                -- Second place: Sword Fight Place - Kill boss and get Swordfighter
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss.Head.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,10,0)
                end
                task.wait(3)
                if workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") then
                    workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").RigType = "R15"
                    workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                end
                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == true
                task.wait()
                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == false
                while task.wait() do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove.CFrame
                        if workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                            fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt"))
                        end
                    end
                end
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                -- First place: Slap Battles - Prepare and teleport
                for i,v in pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("BasePart") and v.CanCollide == true then
                        v.CanCollide = false
                    end
                end
                task.wait(.5)
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(316,40,196)
                end
                task.wait(1)
                game.ReplicatedStorage.RetroAbility:FireServer("Ban Hammer")
                task.wait(2)
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(310,34,191)
                end
                task.wait(2)
                game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local swordfighterScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetSwordfighterExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 117232463555132
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            -- Auto-execute in second place
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss.Head.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,10,0)
                            end
                            task.wait(3)
                            if workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") then
                                workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").RigType = "R15"
                                workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                            end
                            repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == true
                            task.wait()
                            repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == false
                            while task.wait() do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove.CFrame
                                    if workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                                        fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt"))
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then 
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(swordfighterScript) 
                    else 
                        queue_on_teleport(swordfighterScript) 
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeSwordfighterScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function() 
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId) 
            end)
            
            if not success then
                if connection then connection:Disconnect() end
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto Get Tank Glove",

			task.wait(0.3)
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer(unpack({[1]=CFrame.new(17894.3867, -20.5577297, -3562.97974, 0.999158919, -1.34026186e-08, -0.04100601, 1.42693359e-08, 1, 2.08436735e-08, 0.04100601, -2.14112692e-08, 0.999158919);}))

				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Events.PillowEvent:FireServer("AddPillow")
			end
			task.wait(0.3)
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(17894.791, -23.6096096, -3577.8042, -0.999188364, 4.7269662e-08, 0.040281646, 4.80706674e-08, 1, 1.89165021e-08, -0.040281646, 2.08375148e-08, -0.999188364)

			task.wait(0.3)
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 4)
			task.wait(0.3)

			-- Equip Shotgun from inventory

			if not shotgunTool then
				shotgunTool = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Shotgun")

				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(shotgunTool)
			end
			task.wait(0.3)

			-- Auto slap players until 30 coins
			local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
			local Players = game:GetService("Players")
			local reachedTarget = false
			
			while not reachedTarget do
				task.wait(0.1)
				
				-- Check coin count
				local success, coinsText = pcall(function()
					return game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.shotgun_Main.shotgun_hud.coins.Text
				end)
				
				if success and coinsText then
					local coins = tonumber(coinsText:match("%d+")) or 0
					if coins >= 30 then
						reachedTarget = true
						break
					end
				end
				
				-- Get all eligible players (in arena)
				local eligiblePlayers = {}
				for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
					if player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
						table.insert(eligiblePlayers, player)
					end
				end
				
				-- Teleport to random player and slap
				if #eligiblePlayers > 0 then
					local randomPlayer = eligiblePlayers[math.random(1, #eligiblePlayers)]
					if randomPlayer and randomPlayer.Character and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
						-- Teleport with 0.5 second delay
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = randomPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 5)
						task.wait(0.5)
						
						-- Slap the player
						if randomPlayer.Character and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
							local args = { randomPlayer.Character["Right Arm"] }
							ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
						end
					end
				end
			end
			
			task.wait(0.3)

			-- Purchase explosive upgrade
			for i = 1, 2 do
				local args = { "purchase", "explosive" }
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Events"):WaitForChild("shotgun"):FireServer(unpack(args))
			end
			task.wait(0.3)
			
			-- Destroy pillow fort
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(17894.791, -23.6096096, -3577.8042, -0.999188364, 4.7269662e-08, 0.040281646, 4.80706674e-08, 1, 1.89165021e-08, -0.040281646, 2.08375148e-08, -0.999188364)
			repeat 
				task.wait()
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer("explosive")
			until workspace:FindFirstChild(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name.."'s PillowFort") == nil
			
		else
			OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error", Content = "You Dont Own Pillow/50k+ Slaps Required", Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857", Time = 3})
		end
	end
})

	Name = "Anti Void",
	Callback = function()
--ANTI VOID--
if workspace:FindFirstChild("AntiVoid") == nil then
--ANTI VOID--
local Safespot = Instance.new("Part",workspace)
Safespot.Name = "AntiVoid"
Safespot.Position = Vector3.new(-51, -12, 108)
Safespot.Size = Vector3.new(1000000, 1, 1000000)
Safespot.Anchored = true
Safespot.CanCollide = true
Safespot.Transparency = .5
--ANTI VOID--

do
        Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Eggler",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Collect All 10 Eggs",
    Callback = function()
        task.spawn(function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if not player then return end
            
            local character = player.Character
            if not character or not character.Parent then
                character = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
            end
            
            local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then
                hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            end
            
            local EasterEggsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("EasterHuntEggs")
            if not EasterEggsFolder then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "EasterHuntEggs folder not found!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return
            end
            
            -- Create table of all eggs
            local eggs = {
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Black"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Blossom"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Blue"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Brown"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("DarkGrey"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Green"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("LightGrey"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Orange"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Red"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("White")
            }
            
            -- Collect each egg
            for _, egg in pairs(eggs) do
                if egg then
                    pcall(function()
                        -- Find ClickDetector in the egg
                        local clickDetector = egg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
                        
                        if clickDetector then
                            -- Method 1: Teleport to egg and fire ClickDetector
                            local eggPart = egg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") or egg
                            
                            if eggPart then
                                -- Teleport player to the egg
                                hrp.CFrame = eggPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                task.wait(0.05)
                                
                                -- Fire the ClickDetector
                                clickDetector:Click()
                                task.wait(0.03)
                                
                                -- Teleport directly onto the egg for good measure
                                hrp.CFrame = eggPart.CFrame
                                task.wait(0.03)
                                
                                -- Click again to ensure collection
                                clickDetector:Click()
                            end
                        else
                            -- If no ClickDetector, try touching the egg
                            local eggPart = egg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") or egg
                            if eggPart then
                                -- Teleport into the egg multiple times
                                for i = 1, 5 do
                                    hrp.CFrame = eggPart.CFrame
                                    task.wait(0.01)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
                
                task.wait(0.03) -- Wait between eggs
            end
            
            -- Success notification
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success",
                Content = "All eggs collected!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 2
            })
        end)
    end
})

    end
end

do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Slender",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddParagraph("Helper:", [[
Big Thanks To BaconScripter For Helping Me Out For Slender Glove Obtainment Stuff
]])

-- Variables
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

-- Functions
local function equipGlove(gloveName)
    local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
    if not leaderstats then return end
    
    local slaps = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Slaps")
    local currentGlove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
    
    if gloveName == "Balloony" then
        if currentGlove and currentGlove.Value == "Balloony" then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Notice!",
                Content = "You are already equipped Balloony!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        if slaps and slaps.Value < 10500 then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "You don't have enough slaps!",
                Content = "you need 10500 slaps",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        local character = LocalPlayer.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Can't equip Balloony",
                Content = "While in arena!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        local balloony = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and Workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("Balloony")
        if balloony then
            local clickDetector = balloony:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
            if clickDetector then
                fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
            end
        end
    elseif gloveName == "Pocket" then
        if currentGlove and currentGlove.Value == "Pocket" then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "You are already equipped Pocket!",
                Content = "",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        if slaps and slaps.Value < 26000 then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "You don't have enough slaps!",
                Content = "you need 26000 slaps",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        local character = LocalPlayer.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Can't equip Pocket",
                Content = "While in arena!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        local pocket = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and Workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("Pocket")
        if pocket then
            local clickDetector = pocket:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
            if clickDetector then
                fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
            end
        end
    end
end

local function getCode()
    local codeValue = Workspace:FindFirstChild("SecretCodeForPocketKeypad")
    if codeValue then
        local code = codeValue.Value
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Notice!",
            Content = "Code: " .. code,
            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
            Time = 5
        })
        return code
    end
    return nil
end

local function redeemCode()
    local code = getCode()
    if not code then
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Notice!",
            Content = "No code found!",
            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
            Time = 3
        })
        return
    end
    
    for _, room in pairs(Workspace:FindFirstChild("RoomsFolder"):GetChildren() or {}) do
        if string.find(room.Name, "'s Room") then
            local keypad = room:FindFirstChild("PocketKeypad")
            if keypad then
                -- Press reset first
                local resetBtn = keypad:FindFirstChild("Buttons") and keypad.Buttons:FindFirstChild("Reset")
                if resetBtn then
                    local clickDetector = resetBtn:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
                    if clickDetector then
                        fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end
                
                -- Enter each digit
                for i = 1, #code do
                    local digit = string.sub(code, i, i)
                    local button = keypad:FindFirstChild("Buttons") and keypad.Buttons:FindFirstChild(digit)
                    if button then
                        local clickDetector = button:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
                        if clickDetector then
                            fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
                            task.wait(0.3)
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                -- Press enter
                local enterBtn = keypad:FindFirstChild("Buttons") and keypad.Buttons:FindFirstChild("Enter")
                if enterBtn then
                    local clickDetector = enterBtn:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
                    if clickDetector then
                        fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
                    end
                end
                
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Notice!",
                    Content = "Code Redeemed!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                break
            end
        end
    end
end

local function checkTapeRecorder()
    local tapeRecorder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("TapeRecorder")
    if tapeRecorder then
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Notice!",
            Content = "It is spawned!",
            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
            Time = 3
        })
        return true
    else
        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Notice!",
            Content = "Not spawned yet, use Balloony",
            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
            Time = 3
        })
        return false
    end
end

local function interactWithTapeRecorder()
    local tapeRecorder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("TapeRecorder")
    if tapeRecorder then
        local front = tapeRecorder:FindFirstChild("Front")
        if front then
            local prompt = front:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt")
            if prompt then
                fireproximityprompt(prompt)
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end
    end
end

local function collectAllPages()
    local bountyRoom = Workspace:FindFirstChild("BountyHunterRoom")
    if bountyRoom then
        local mysteryRoom = bountyRoom:FindFirstChild("BountyHunterMysteryRoom")
        if mysteryRoom then
            local pages = mysteryRoom:FindFirstChild("Pages")
            if pages then
                for _, page in pairs(pages:GetChildren()) do
                    local clickDetector = page:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
                    if clickDetector then
                        fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
                        task.wait(0.2)
                    end
                end
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Notice!",
                    Content = "Pages Collected!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
            end
        end
    end
end

	PremiumOnly = false

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Find & Teleport To Painting",
    Callback = function()
        local paintingModel = nil
        
        -- Search entire workspace for PaintingModel
        for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
            if obj:IsA("Model") and obj.Name == "PaintingModel" then
                paintingModel = obj
                break
            end
        end
        
        -- If found, teleport to it
        if paintingModel then
            local character = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character
            local hrp = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            
            if hrp then
                local part = paintingModel:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") or paintingModel.PrimaryPart
                if part then
                    hrp.CFrame = part.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Success",
                        Content = "Teleported to PaintingModel!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                else
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Error",
                        Content = "PaintingModel found but has no BasePart!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        else
            -- Notify if not found
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Not Found",
                Content = "PaintingModel not found in workspace!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

end

Tab:AddButton({

fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Adios"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Someone Using Car Keys?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Car Keys" then
                    found = true
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Car Keys glove.",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Car Keys glove",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Car Keys Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Car Keys" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Car Keys Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("AdiosActivated"):FireServer()

do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Suction",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Suction Button with Auto-Execute
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Obby Place + Get Suction",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 89837553336708
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        
        local function executeSuctionScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetSuctionExecuted then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetSuctionExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                -- Second place: Obby Place - Load the suction script
                loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://pastefy.app/faY5eqRD/raw'))()
                
            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlayId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                -- First place: Slap Battles - Click plungers and teleport
                if workspace:FindFirstChild("BountyHunterRoom") and workspace.BountyHunterRoom:FindFirstChild("PlungerMain") and workspace.BountyHunterRoom.PlungerMain:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                    fireclickdetector(workspace.BountyHunterRoom.PlungerMain.ClickDetector)
                end
                
                if workspace:FindFirstChild("plungers") and workspace.plungers:FindFirstChild("ToiletPlunger") and workspace.plungers.ToiletPlunger:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                    fireclickdetector(workspace.plungers.ToiletPlunger.ClickDetector)
                end
                
                task.wait(2)
                game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)
            end
        end

        -- Function to set up teleport monitoring
        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local suctionScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetSuctionExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 89837553336708
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            -- Auto-execute in second place
                            loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://pastefy.app/faY5eqRD/raw'))()
                        end
                    ]]
                    
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then 
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(suctionScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(suctionScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        -- Main execution logic
        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeSuctionScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            
            if not success then
                if connection then
                    connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

end
