Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Equip Hitman (Sharp Shooter/Court Evidence Badges Need)",
    Callback = function()
fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Hitman"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
	Callback = function()   
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Hitman" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Left Leg"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                [2] = false  -- The second argument, set to false as in your original script
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Left Leg" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.HitmanHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Hitman",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end
do
    Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Debug",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

-- Shared variable to store the code
local debugCode = nil

-- First Button: Get Code and store it
Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Get Code",
	Callback = function()
		local code = ""

		-- Path 1: Count "Duck" MeshParts
		local success1, duckCount = pcall(function()
			local ducks = workspace["Debug Room"].DuckTable.DuckTable:GetChildren()
			local count = 0
			for _, obj in ipairs(ducks) do
				if obj:IsA("MeshPart") and obj.Name == "Duck" then
					count += 1
				end
			end
			return count
		end)
		code = code .. (success1 and tostring(duckCount) or "?")

		-- Path 2: AdminNumber Text
		local success2, adminNum = pcall(function()
			local text = workspace["Debug Room"].AdminGloves.GlovesCode.SurfaceGui.AdminNumber.Text
			return tonumber(text) or 0
		end)
		code = code .. (success2 and tostring(adminNum) or "?")

		-- Path 3: MazeNumber Text
		local success3, mazeNum = pcall(function()
			local text = workspace["Debug Room"].Maze.MazePrize.SurfaceGui.MazeNumber.Text
			return tonumber(text) or 0
		end)
		code = code .. (success3 and tostring(mazeNum) or "?")

		-- Path 4: Always 7 (game changed to make last digit always 7)
		local responseNum = 7
		code = code .. tostring(responseNum)

		-- Store code globally
		debugCode = code

		-- Show notification with debug info
		OrionLib:MakeNotification({
			Name = "Code Checker",
			Content = "The Debug Glove Code is: " .. code,
			Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
			Time = 5
		})
		
		-- Print debug info to console
		print("Debug Code Found: " .. code)
		print("Path 1 (Ducks): " .. (success1 and tostring(duckCount) or "FAILED"))
		print("Path 2 (Admin): " .. (success2 and tostring(adminNum) or "FAILED"))
		print("Path 3 (Maze): " .. (success3 and tostring(mazeNum) or "FAILED"))
		print("Path 4 (Fixed): 7")
	end
})

-- Second Button: Use code to press keypad buttons
Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Claim Debug Glove",
	Callback = function()
		if not debugCode or string.find(debugCode, "?") then
			OrionLib:MakeNotification({
				Name = "Error",
				Content = "Code not found or incomplete. Please run the first button again.",
				Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
				Time = 4
			})
			return
		end

		local buttonsModel = workspace["Debug Room"].Keypad.Buttons

		-- Press each number's part
		for digit in debugCode:gmatch("%d") do
			local buttonPart = buttonsModel:FindFirstChild(digit)
			if buttonPart then
				local clickDetector = buttonPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
				if clickDetector then
					fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
					wait(0.2) -- small delay to avoid overlaps
				end
			end
		end

		-- Press Enter
		local enterPart = buttonsModel:FindFirstChild("Enter")
		if enterPart then
			local enterClick = enterPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
			if enterClick then
				fireclickdetector(enterClick)
			end
		end
		
		OrionLib:MakeNotification({
			Name = "Success",
			Content = "Code entered: " .. debugCode,
			Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
			Time = 4
		})
	end
})

end

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Auto Slap Aura Players",

        -- Define glove configurations
        local gloveConfigs = {
            ["Rage"] = {
                remoteName = "GRRRR",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                            [2] = false
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.GRRRR:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Eggler"] = {
                remoteName = "GeneralHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {
                                    -- Add Eggler-specific arguments here
                                }
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Fan"] = {
                remoteName = "GeneralHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {
                                    -- Add Fan-specific arguments here
                                }
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Scythe"] = {
                remoteName = "GeneralHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {
                                    -- Add Scythe-specific arguments here
                                }
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Snow"] = {
                remoteName = "SnowHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {
                                    -- Add Snow-specific arguments here
                                }
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.SnowHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            }
        }
        
        local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
        local Players = game:GetService("Players")
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        
        -- Get current equipped glove
        local equippedGlove = localPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value
        
        -- Check if equipped glove is in our supported list
        if not gloveConfigs[equippedGlove] then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Equip one of: Rage, Eggler, Fan, Scythe, or Snow",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        -- Get the config for current glove
        local gloveConfig = gloveConfigs[equippedGlove]
        
        -- Start the loop
        while true do
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= localPlayer then
                    gloveConfig.action(player)
                end
            end
            wait(0.5)
        end
    end
})

end

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Tableflip Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Tableflip" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)) -- Teleport above

            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Tableflip Player Not Found",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Anti Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AntiRagdoll = Value

        while _G.AntiRagdoll do
            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                if char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and char.Ragdolled.Value == true then
                    local torso = char:FindFirstChild("Torso")
                    if torso then
                        torso.Anchored = true
                        repeat task.wait() until char.Ragdolled.Value == false
                        torso.Anchored = false
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
	Name = "Anti Void",
	Callback = function()
--ANTI VOID--
if workspace:FindFirstChild("AntiVoid") == nil then
--ANTI VOID--
local Safespot = Instance.new("Part",workspace)
Safespot.Name = "AntiVoid"
Safespot.Position = Vector3.new(-51, -12, 108)
Safespot.Size = Vector3.new(1000000, 1, 1000000)
Safespot.Anchored = true
Safespot.CanCollide = true
Safespot.Transparency = .5
--ANTI VOID--
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Success",Content = "Created Successfully!",Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",Time = 3})
else
game.workspace.AntiVoid:Destroy()
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Success",Content = "Removed Successfully!",Image = "rbxassetid://7733715400",Time = 3})
end
end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Oven",
    Callback = function()
        -- Get the local player
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local playerName = localPlayer.Name
        
        -- Try to find oven with player's name pattern
        local ovenModel = workspace:FindFirstChild(playerName .. "'s Oven")
        
        -- If not found with exact name, try to find any oven that contains the player's name
        if not ovenModel then
            for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("Model") and obj.Name:find(playerName) and obj.Name:find("Oven") then
                    ovenModel = obj
                    break
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- If still not found, try to find any oven model
        if not ovenModel then
            for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("Model") and obj.Name:find("Oven") then
                    ovenModel = obj
                    break
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- If oven found, find hitbox and teleport
        if ovenModel then
            local hitbox = ovenModel:FindFirstChild("Hitbox")
            
            -- If Hitbox not found directly, search deeper
            if not hitbox then
                hitbox = ovenModel:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
            end
            
            if hitbox then
                local character = localPlayer.Character
                if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    -- Teleport to hitbox position
                    character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = hitbox.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0) -- Slightly above the hitbox
                  end
	    end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Slapple Island",
    Callback = function()
game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-391, 51, 1)
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Place Birthday Cake",
    Callback = function()
        -- Get the local player
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        
        -- Look for Birthday Cake in backpack
        local cakeTool = nil
        for _, item in pairs(localPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
            if item:IsA("Tool") and item.Name == "Birthday Cake" then
                cakeTool = item
                break
            end
        end
        
        if cakeTool then
            -- Equip the cake tool
            localPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(cakeTool)
            
            -- Small delay to ensure tool is equipped
            task.wait(0.3)
            
            -- Find the CakePromptPlacement and its proximity prompt
            local success = false
            local island5 = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena") and workspace.Arena:FindFirstChild("island5")
            
            if island5 then
                -- Search for any BasePart named Union.CakePromptPlacement
                for _, part in pairs(island5:GetDescendants()) do
                    if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Name == "Union.CakePromptPlacement" then
                        -- Look for CakeProximityPrompt inside
                        local prompt = part:FindFirstChild("CakeProximityPrompt")
                        if prompt and prompt:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                            -- Fire the proximity prompt
                            prompt:InputHoldBegin()
                            task.wait(0.1)
                            prompt:InputHoldEnd()
                            
                            success = true

                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Quake Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Quake" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Right Arm"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Right Arm"]
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Right Arm" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Quake",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end
do
Tab = Window:MakeTab({
	Name = "Shellbert",
	Icon = "rbxassetid://7733673987",
	PremiumOnly = false
	})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Collect All 10 Eggs",
    Callback = function()
        task.spawn(function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if not player then return end
            
            local character = player.Character
            if not character or not character.Parent then
                character = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
            end
            
            local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then
                hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            end
            
            local EasterEggsFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("EasterHuntEggs")
            if not EasterEggsFolder then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "EasterHuntEggs folder not found!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return
            end
            
            -- Create table of all eggs
            local eggs = {
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Black"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Blossom"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Blue"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Brown"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("DarkGrey"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Green"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("LightGrey"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Orange"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("Red"),
                EasterEggsFolder:FindFirstChild("White")
            }
            
            -- Collect each egg
            for _, egg in pairs(eggs) do
                if egg then
                    pcall(function()
                        -- Find ClickDetector in the egg
                        local clickDetector = egg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
                        
                        if clickDetector then
                            -- Method 1: Teleport to egg and fire ClickDetector
                            local eggPart = egg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") or egg
                            
                            if eggPart then
                                -- Teleport player to the egg
                                hrp.CFrame = eggPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                task.wait(0.05)
                                
                                -- Fire the ClickDetector
                                clickDetector:Click()
                                task.wait(0.03)
                                
                                -- Teleport directly onto the egg for good measure
                                hrp.CFrame = eggPart.CFrame
                                task.wait(0.03)
                                
                                -- Click again to ensure collection
                                clickDetector:Click()
                            end
                        else
                            -- If no ClickDetector, try touching the egg
                            local eggPart = egg:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") or egg
                            if eggPart then
                                -- Teleport into the egg multiple times
                                for i = 1, 5 do
                                    hrp.CFrame = eggPart.CFrame
                                    task.wait(0.01)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
                
                task.wait(0.03) -- Wait between eggs
            end
            
            -- Success notification
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success",
                Content = "All eggs collected!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 2
            })
        end)
    end
})

end
end

local WalkFlingActive = false
local WalkFlingConnection = nil
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

-- Get HumanoidRootPart
local function getRoot(char)
    return char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
end

-- Enable noclip
local function setNoclip(enabled)
    local character = player.Character
    if character then
        for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                part.CanCollide = not enabled
            end
        end
    end
end

-- WalkFling loop
local function startWalkFling()
    if WalkFlingConnection then return end
    
    WalkFlingConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not WalkFlingActive then return end
        
        local character = player.Character
        local root = getRoot(character)
        local vel = nil
        local movel = 0.1
        
        -- Wait for valid character
        while not (character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent) do
            RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
            character = player.Character
            root = getRoot(character)
        end
        
        -- Store velocity and apply fling
        vel = root.Velocity
        root.Velocity = vel * 10000 + Vector3.new(0, 10000, 0)
        
        -- Enable noclip while flinging
        setNoclip(true)
        
        -- Restore velocity after a tick
        RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
        if character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent then
            root.Velocity = vel
        end
        
        -- Add oscillating force
        RunService.Stepped:Wait()
        if character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent then
            root.Velocity = vel + Vector3.new(0, movel, 0)
            movel = movel * -1
        end
    end)
end

local function stopWalkFling()
    WalkFlingActive = false
    if WalkFlingConnection then
        WalkFlingConnection:Disconnect()
        WalkFlingConnection = nil
    end
    setNoclip(false)
end

-- Auto-disable on death
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    task.wait(0.1)
    if WalkFlingActive then
        stopWalkFling()
        task.wait(0.1)
        WalkFlingActive = true
        startWalkFling()
    end
end)

-- Orion Hub Toggle
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "WalkFling",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            WalkFlingActive = true
            startWalkFling()
        else
            stopWalkFling()
        end
    end
})

end

            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            
            -- Check if PlayerData folder exists
            local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("PlayerData", 5)
            if not playerData then

                return
            end
            
            -- Check if player folder exists
            local playerFolder = playerData:WaitForChild(playerName, 5)
            if not playerFolder then

                return
            end
            
            -- Check if NullShards StringValue exists
            local nullShardsValue = playerFolder:WaitForChild("NullShards", 5)
            if not nullShardsValue then

                return
            end
            
            -- Verify it's a StringValue
            if nullShardsValue.ClassName ~= "StringValue" then

                return
            end
            
            -- Set the value
            local oldValue = nullShardsValue.Value
            nullShardsValue.Value = getgenv().nullshardChanger
            
            
            print("[Null Shards] Changed from " .. oldValue .. " to " .. getgenv().nullshardChanger)
            
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({

-- Variables
local deathSoundEnabled = false
local currentSoundId = ""
local monitorConnection = nil
local childAddedConnections = {}

-- Function to clean up old connections
local function cleanupConnections()
    if monitorConnection then
        monitorConnection:Disconnect()
        monitorConnection = nil
    end
    
    for _, conn in pairs(childAddedConnections) do
        pcall(function()
            conn:Disconnect()
        end)
    end
    childAddedConnections = {}
end

-- Function to modify death sounds in a character
local function modifyDeathSounds(character)
    if not deathSoundEnabled then return end
    if not character then return end
    
    local torso = character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
    if not torso then return end
    
    for _, sound in pairs(torso:GetChildren()) do
        if sound:IsA("Sound") then
            local soundName = sound.Name:lower()
            if soundName:find("death") or soundName:find("die") then
                pcall(function()
                    if sound.SoundId ~= currentSoundId then
                        sound.SoundId = currentSoundId
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Function to setup listener for new sounds
local function setupSoundListener(character)
    if not character then return end
    
    local torso = character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
    if not torso then return end
    
    local connection = torso.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA("Sound") and deathSoundEnabled then
            local soundName = child.Name:lower()
            if soundName:find("death") or soundName:find("die") then
                task.wait(0.1)
                pcall(function()
                    child.SoundId = currentSoundId
                end)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    table.insert(childAddedConnections, connection)
end

-- Function to start monitoring
local function startMonitoring()
    if monitorConnection then return end
    
    monitorConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if deathSoundEnabled then
            local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if character then
                modifyDeathSounds(character)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    -- Setup listener for current character
    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    if character then
        setupSoundListener(character)
    end
end

-- Function to stop monitoring
local function stopMonitoring()
    cleanupConnections()
end

-- Function to update all existing death sounds
local function updateAllDeathSounds()
    if not deathSoundEnabled then return end
    
    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    if character then
        local torso = character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
        if torso then
            for _, sound in pairs(torso:GetChildren()) do
                if sound:IsA("Sound") then
                    local soundName = sound.Name:lower()
                    if soundName:find("death") or soundName:find("die") then
                        pcall(function()
                            sound.SoundId = currentSoundId
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Add Sound ID TextBox
Tab:AddParagraph("Custom Sound ID:", "Enter your sound ID below (format: rbxassetid://1234567890)")

local soundIdBox = Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "Put Custom Sound ID",
    Default = currentSoundId,
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(value)
        if value and value ~= "" then
            -- Ensure it has rbxassetid:// prefix if not present
            if not value:find("rbxassetid://") then
                currentSoundId = "rbxassetid://" .. value
            else
                currentSoundId = value
            end
            
            -- Update existing sounds if enabled
            if deathSoundEnabled then
                updateAllDeathSounds()
            end
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Sound ID Updated",
                Content = "New sound ID: " .. currentSoundId,
                Time = 2
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Add Toggle for auto apply
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Apply Death Sound",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(value)
        deathSoundEnabled = value
        
        if value then
            startMonitoring()
            updateAllDeathSounds()
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Death Sound Modifier",
                Content = "Enabled! Death sounds will be changed to: " .. currentSoundId,
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            stopMonitoring()
            
        end
    end
})

-- Handle character respawn
game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
    task.wait(0.5)
    
    if deathSoundEnabled then
        setupSoundListener(character)
        task.wait(0.2)
        modifyDeathSounds(character)
    end
end)

-- Initial setup
startMonitoring()

local nametagText = ""
local autoNametag = false
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "Type Ur Own Any Nametag",
    Default = "",
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        nametagText = Value
    end
})

-- Button to apply nametag once
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Change Nametag",
    Callback = function()
        if nametagText == "" then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Please enter text in the textbox first!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        -- Find and update nametag
        local character = player.Character
        if character then
            local nametag = character:FindFirstChild("Head") and character.Head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
            if nametag then
                local topLabel = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels") and nametag.Labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
                if topLabel then
                    topLabel.Text = nametagText
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Success",
                        Content = "Nametag changed to: " .. nametagText,
                        Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                else
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Error",
                        Content = "TopLabel not found!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                end
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Nametag not found!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
            end
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Character not found!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Toggle for auto nametag
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Change Nametag",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoNametag = Value
        if Value then
            -- Start auto nametag loop
            task.spawn(function()
                while autoNametag do
                    if nametagText ~= "" then
                        local character = player.Character
                        if character then
                            local nametag = character:FindFirstChild("Head") and character.Head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
                            if nametag then
                                local topLabel = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels") and nametag.Labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
                                if topLabel then
                                    topLabel.Text = nametagText
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    task.wait(0.01)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

-- Auto reapply nametag when character respawns
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
    if autoNametag and nametagText ~= "" then
        -- Wait for character to fully load
        wait(2)
        local nametag = character:FindFirstChild("Head") and character.Head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
        if nametag then
            local topLabel = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels") and nametag.Labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
            if topLabel then
                topLabel.Text = nametagText
            end
        end
    end
end)

        -- P2W Gloves
        ["OVERKILL"] = ReplicatedStorage.Overkillhit,
        ["Spectator"] = ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit,
        ["CUSTOM"] = ReplicatedStorage.CustomHit,
        ["Ultra Instinct"] = ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit,
        
        -- Other Gloves
        ["spin"] = ReplicatedStorage.spinhit,
        ["Stick"] = ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit,
        ["potato"] = ReplicatedStorage.potatohit,
        ["Error"] = ReplicatedStorage.Errorhit,
        ["killerfish"] = ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit,
        ["Titan"] = ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit,
        ["Acrobat"] = ReplicatedStorage.AcHit,
        
        -- Fallback for unknown gloves
        ["GeneralHit"] = ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit,
        ["b"] = ReplicatedStorage.b,
        ["HtStun"] = ReplicatedStorage.HtStun
    }
    
    -- Add metatable for dynamic glove lookups
    setmetatable(gloveHits, {
        __index = function(t, key)
            -- Try to find any remote that matches the glove name
            for _, child in pairs(ReplicatedStorage:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                    local childName = child.Name:lower()
                    local gloveName = tostring(key):lower()
                    
                    if childName == gloveName or
                       childName == gloveName .. "hit" or
                       childName == "ht" .. gloveName or
                       childName:find(gloveName, 1, true) then
                        rawset(t, key, child) -- Cache for next time
                        return child
                    end
                end
            end
            
            -- Ultimate fallback - first available remote
            for _, child in pairs(ReplicatedStorage:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                    rawset(t, key, child) -- Cache for next time
                    return child
                end
            end
            
            return nil
        end
    })
    
    -- Function to get current glove
    local function getCurrentGlove()
        local success, result = pcall(function()
            if localPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats") then
                local gloveValue = localPlayer.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if gloveValue then
                    return gloveValue.Value
                end
            end
            return "Default"
        end)
        
        if success then
            return result
        end
        return "Default"
    end
    
    -- Function to get the remote for a glove
    local function getGloveRemote(gloveName)
        -- Try direct lookup from gloveHits
        local remote = gloveHits[gloveName]
        
        if remote and typeof(remote) == "Instance" and remote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
            return remote
        end
        
        -- If we get here, the metatable will handle it
        return gloveHits[gloveName]
    end
    
    -- Create slider
    local slapAuraSpeed = Tab:AddSlider({
        Name = "Slap Aura Speed",
        Min = 0.1,
        Max = 2,
        Default = 0.5,
        Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
        Increment = 0.1,
        ValueName = "seconds",
        Callback = function(Value)
            currentCooldown = Value
        end
    })
    
    -- Create toggle
    Tab:AddToggle({
        Name = "Slap Aura",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(enabled)
            -- Prevent random "Slap Aura Disabled" popups
            if isSlapAuraEnabled == enabled then
                return
            end
            
            isSlapAuraEnabled = enabled
            
            if enabled then
                -- Disconnect existing connection
                if slapAuraConnection then
                    slapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnection = nil
                end
                
                -- Get current glove
                local currentGlove = getCurrentGlove()
                
                -- Get the remote for this glove
                local remote = getGloveRemote(currentGlove)
                
                if not remote then
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Slap Aura Error",
                        Content = "No remote found for glove: " .. currentGlove,
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                    isSlapAuraEnabled = false
                    return
                end
                
                print("Slap Aura: Enabled with glove '" .. currentGlove .. "' using remote '" .. remote.Name .. "'")
                
                -- Start slap aura
                slapAuraConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                    local currentTime = tick()
                    
                    -- Check cooldown
                    if currentTime - lastHitTime < currentCooldown then
                        return
                    end
                    
                    -- Check if still enabled and has character
                    if not isSlapAuraEnabled or not localPlayer.Character then
                        return
                    end
                    
                    -- Get local character position
                    local localChar = localPlayer.Character
                    local localRoot = localChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if not localRoot then
                        return
                    end
                    
                    -- Find players to slap
                    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                            local char = player.Character
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                            local torso = char:FindFirstChild("Torso") or char:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
                            
                            -- Check if valid target
                            if torso and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                -- Optional distance check (40 studs max)
                                local playerRoot = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if playerRoot then
                                    local distance = (playerRoot.Position - localRoot.Position).Magnitude
                                    if distance > 40 then
                                        continue
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                -- Fire the remote
                                local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                                    remote:FireServer(torso)
                                end)
                                
                                if success then
                                    lastHitTime = currentTime
                                    break -- Hit one player per cycle
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Slap Aura Enabled",
                    Content = "Glove: " .. currentGlove,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 3
                })
                
            else
                -- Disable
                if slapAuraConnection then
                    slapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnection = nil
                end
                
                -- Only show notification if it was previously enabled
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Slap Aura Disabled",
                    Content = "",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })
end
    
Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Safespot Stuff"
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Create Safespot",
    Callback = function()
        if workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot") == nil then
            local Safespot = Instance.new("Model", workspace)
            Safespot.Name = "Safespot"

            local base = Instance.new("Part")
            base.Name = "Base"
            base.Size = Vector3.new(500, 10, 500)
            base.Position = Vector3.new(10000, -50, 10000)
            base.Anchored = true
            base.CanCollide = true
            base.Transparency = 0.5
            base.Parent = Safespot

            local partsData = {
                {"DefendPart",  Vector3.new(500, 117, 5),   Vector3.new(10000.2, 13, 9752.45)},
                {"DefendPart1", Vector3.new(5, 117, 496),   Vector3.new(10248.2, 13, 10002.4)},
                {"DefendPart2", Vector3.new(497, 117, 6),   Vector3.new(9998.13, 13, 10247.2)},
                {"DefendPart3", Vector3.new(7, 117, 490),   Vector3.new(9752.71, 13, 9999.28)},
                {"DefendPart4", Vector3.new(491, 10, 491),  Vector3.new(10001.1, 76, 9999.66)},
            }

            for _, partInfo in pairs(partsData) do
                local part = Instance.new("Part")
                part.Name = partInfo[1]
                part.Size = partInfo[2]
                part.Position = partInfo[3]
                part.Anchored = true
                part.CanCollide = true
                part.Transparency = 0.5
                part.Parent = Safespot
            end
        end

        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Checker",
            Content = "Created Successfully!",
            Image = "rbxassetid://7733919427",
            Time = 3
        })
    end
})

-- Add section for Ghost On/Off
Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Ghost On/Off"
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Ghost Invisibility",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        local hasGhost = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats") and
                         game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and
                         game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Ghost"

        if Value == true then
            if hasGhost then
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Ghostinvisibilityactivated:FireServer()
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Ghost Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
            end
        elseif Value == false and hasGhost then
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Ghostinvisibilitydeactivated:FireServer()
        end
    end
})

    Name = "Server Settings"
})

    end
})

-- ServerHop (Regular Server)
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "ServerHop (Regular Server)",
    Callback = function()
        local PlaceID = game.PlaceId
        local AllIDs = {}
        local foundAnything = ""
        local actualHour = os.date("!*t").hour
        local Deleted = false

        local success, data = pcall(function()
            return game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONDecode(readfile("NotSameServers.json"))
        end)
        if success then
            AllIDs = data
        else
            table.insert(AllIDs, actualHour)
            writefile("NotSameServers.json", game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONEncode(AllIDs))
        end

        local function TPReturner()
            local Site
            if foundAnything == "" then
                Site = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. PlaceID .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100'))
            else
                Site = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. PlaceID .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor=' .. foundAnything))
            end

            if Site.nextPageCursor and Site.nextPageCursor ~= "null" and Site.nextPageCursor ~= nil then
                foundAnything = Site.nextPageCursor
            end

            for i, v in pairs(Site.data) do
                local Possible = true
                local ID = tostring(v.id)
                if tonumber(v.maxPlayers) > tonumber(v.playing) then
                    for _, Existing in pairs(AllIDs) do
                        if ID == tostring(Existing) then
                            Possible = false
                            break
                        end
                    end
                    if Possible then
                        table.insert(AllIDs, ID)
                        wait()
                        pcall(function()
                            writefile("NotSameServers.json", game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONEncode(AllIDs))
                            wait()
                            game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(PlaceID, ID, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                        end)
                        wait(4)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function Teleport()
            while wait() do
                pcall(function()
                    TPReturner()
                    if foundAnything ~= "" then
                        TPReturner()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        -- Start teleporting to new servers
        Teleport()
    end
})

-- ServerHop (Small Server)
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "ServerHop (Small Server)",
    Callback = function()
        local Http = game:GetService("HttpService")
        local TPS = game:GetService("TeleportService")
        local Api = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"
        local place = game.PlaceId
        local serversUrl = Api .. place .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"

        local function ListServers(cursor)
            local Raw = game:HttpGet(serversUrl .. ((cursor and "&cursor=" .. cursor) or ""))
            return Http:JSONDecode(Raw)
        end

        local Server, Next
        repeat
            local Servers = ListServers(Next)
            Server = Servers.data[1]
            Next = Servers.nextPageCursor
        until Server

        TPS:TeleportToPlaceInstance(place, Server.id, game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer)
    end
})

    Name = "Kick/Reset If Stuck"
})

    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Arena Settings"
})

-- Auto Enter Arena System
local AutoEnterActive = false
local AutoEnterMode = "Arena" -- Default mode

Tab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Enter",
    Default = "Arena",
    Options = {"Arena", "Arena Default"},
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoEnterMode = Value
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Enter",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoEnterActive = Value
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while AutoEnterActive do
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if not player then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then 
                    task.wait(0.5) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                -- Check if already entered
                local entered = character:FindFirstChild("entered")
                
                if not entered then
                    -- Get the correct teleport part based on mode
                    local teleportFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby")
                    if not teleportFolder then
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        continue
                    end
                    
                    local teleportPart = nil
                    
                    if AutoEnterMode == "Arena" then
                        teleportPart = teleportFolder:FindFirstChild("Teleport1")
                    elseif AutoEnterMode == "Arena Default" then
                        teleportPart = teleportFolder:FindFirstChild("Teleport2")
                    end
                    
                    if teleportPart then
                        pcall(function()
                            -- Method 1: Teleport player directly to the teleport part
                            local touchPart = nil
                            
                            -- Find the actual part to teleport to
                            if teleportPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                                touchPart = teleportPart
                            else
                                touchPart = teleportPart:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
                            end
                            
                            if touchPart then
                                -- Teleport player to the teleport location
                                hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                -- Move directly into the teleport part
                                hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                -- Spam teleport into the part to ensure trigger
                                for i = 1, 5 do
                                    hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame
                                    task.wait(0.01)
                                end
                                
                                -- Move slightly forward through the teleport
                                hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame + touchPart.CFrame.LookVector * 3
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                -- Teleport back and forth through the teleport
                                for i = 1, 3 do
                                    hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame - touchPart.CFrame.LookVector * 2
                                    task.wait(0.05)
                                    hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame + touchPart.CFrame.LookVector * 4
                                    task.wait(0.05)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                else
                    -- Already entered, just wait
                    task.wait(1)
                end
                
                -- Wait before next attempt
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Arena",
    Callback = function()
        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new()
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Default Arena",
    Callback = function()
        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(122, 360, -3)
        end
    end
})
